<p dir="auto"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">åˆ†ç±»æ˜¯é¥æ„Ÿæ•°æ®åˆ†æä¸­çš„ä¸€é¡¹åŸºæœ¬ä»»åŠ¡ï¼Œå…¶ç›®æ ‡æ˜¯ä¸ºæ¯å¹…å›¾åƒåˆ†é…è¯­ä¹‰æ ‡ç­¾ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚â€œåŸå¸‚â€ã€â€œæ£®æ—â€ã€â€œå†œç”°â€ç­‰ã€‚ä¸ºå›¾åƒåˆ†é…æ ‡ç­¾çš„è¿‡ç¨‹æ˜¯ç§°ä¸ºå›¾åƒçº§åˆ†ç±»ã€‚</font><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">ç„¶è€Œï¼Œåœ¨æŸäº›æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œå•ä¸ªå›¾åƒå¯èƒ½åŒ…å«å¤šç§ä¸åŒçš„åœŸåœ°è¦†ç›–ç±»å‹ï¼Œä¾‹å¦‚æœ‰æ²³æµç©¿è¿‡çš„æ£®æ—ï¼Œæˆ–è€…æ—¢æœ‰ä½å®…åŒºåˆæœ‰å•†ä¸šåŒºçš„åŸå¸‚ã€‚</font><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">åœ¨è¿™äº›æƒ…å†µä¸‹ï¼Œå›¾åƒçº§åˆ†ç±»å˜å¾—æ›´åŠ å¤æ‚ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”æ¶‰åŠä¸ºå•ä¸ªå›¾åƒåˆ†é…å¤šä¸ªæ ‡ç­¾ã€‚</font><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">è¿™å¯ä»¥é€šè¿‡ç»“åˆç‰¹å¾æå–å’Œæœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ ç®—æ³•æ¥å‡†ç¡®è¯†åˆ«ä¸åŒçš„åœŸåœ°è¦†ç›–ç±»å‹æ¥å®ç°ã€‚</font><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">éœ€è¦æ³¨æ„çš„æ˜¯ï¼Œå›¾åƒçº§åˆ†ç±»ä¸åº”ä¸åƒç´ çº§åˆ†ç±»ï¼ˆä¹Ÿç§°ä¸ºè¯­ä¹‰åˆ†å‰²ï¼‰æ··æ·†ã€‚</font><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å›¾åƒçº§åˆ†ç±»ä¸ºæ•´ä¸ªå›¾åƒåˆ†é…å•ä¸ªæ ‡ç­¾ï¼Œè€Œè¯­ä¹‰åˆ†å‰²ä¸ºå›¾åƒä¸­çš„æ¯ä¸ªå•ç‹¬åƒç´ åˆ†é…ä¸€ä¸ªæ ‡ç­¾ï¼Œä»è€Œå¯¹å›¾åƒä¸­çš„åœŸåœ°è¦†ç›–ç±»å‹è¿›è¡Œé«˜åº¦è¯¦ç»†ä¸”å‡†ç¡®çš„è¡¨ç¤ºã€‚</font><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">é˜…è¯»</font></font><a href="https://medium.com/@robmarkcole/a-brief-introduction-to-satellite-image-classification-with-neural-networks-3ce28be15683" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">ç¥ç»ç½‘ç»œå«æ˜Ÿå›¾åƒåˆ†ç±»ç®€ä»‹</font></font></a></p>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation</h2><a id="user-content-segmentation" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼š ç»†åˆ†" href="#segmentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/segmentation.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/segmentation.png" width="500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>(left) a satellite image and (right) the semantic classes in the image.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Image segmentation is a crucial step in image analysis and computer vision, with the goal of dividing an image into semantically meaningful segments or regions. The process of image segmentation assigns a class label to each pixel in an image, effectively transforming an image from a 2D grid of pixels into a 2D grid of pixels with assigned class labels. One common application of image segmentation is road or building segmentation, where the goal is to identify and separate roads and buildings from other features within an image. To accomplish this task, single class models are often trained to differentiate between roads and background, or buildings and background. These models are designed to recognize specific features, such as color, texture, and shape, that are characteristic of roads or buildings, and use this information to assign class labels to the pixels in an image. Another common application of image segmentation is land use or crop type classification, where the goal is to identify and map different land cover types within an image. In this case, multi-class models are typically used to recognize and differentiate between multiple classes within an image, such as forests, urban areas, and agricultural land. These models are capable of recognizing complex relationships between different land cover types, allowing for a more comprehensive understanding of the image content. Read <a href="https://medium.com/@robmarkcole/a-brief-introduction-to-satellite-image-segmentation-with-neural-networks-33ea732d5bce" rel="nofollow">A brief introduction to satellite image segmentation with neural networks</a>. <strong>Note</strong> that many articles which refer to 'hyperspectral land classification' are often actually describing semantic segmentation. <a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/semantic-segmentation-of-aerial-imagery-using-u-net-in-python-552705238514" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation - Land use &amp; land cover</h3><a id="user-content-segmentation---land-use--land-cover" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç»†åˆ† - åœŸåœ°åˆ©ç”¨å’ŒåœŸåœ°è¦†ç›–" href="#segmentation---land-use--land-cover"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation - Vegetation, deforestation, crops &amp; crop boundaries</h3><a id="user-content-segmentation---vegetation-deforestation-crops--crop-boundaries" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šåˆ†å‰² - æ¤è¢«ã€æ£®æ—ç ä¼ã€å†œä½œç‰©å’Œå†œä½œç‰©è¾¹ç•Œ" href="#segmentation---vegetation-deforestation-crops--crop-boundaries"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Note that deforestation detection may be treated as a segmentation task or a change detection task</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/geekculture/%D1%81r%D0%BE%D1%80-field-boundary-detection-approaches-and-main-challenges-46e37dd276bc" rel="nofollow">Ğ¡rĞ¾Ñ€ field boundary detection: approaches and main challenges</a> -&gt; Medium article, covering historical and modern approaches</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/nasaharvest/kenya-crop-mask">kenya-crop-mask</a> -&gt; Annual and in-season crop mapping in Kenya - LSTM classifier to classify pixels as containing crop or not, and a multi-spectral forecaster that provides a 12 month time series given a partial input. Dataset downloaded from GEE and pytorch lightning used for training</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/whats-growing-there-a5618a2e6933" rel="nofollow">Whatâ€™s growing there? Identify crops from multi-spectral remote sensing data (Sentinel 2)</a> using eo-learn for data pre-processing, cloud detection, NDVI calculation, image augmentation &amp; fastai</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jaeeolma/tree-detection-evo">Tree species classification from from airborne LiDAR and hyperspectral data using 3D convolutional neural networks</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/nerd-for-tech/crop-type-classification-cf5cc2593396" rel="nofollow">crop-type-classification</a> -&gt; using Sentinel 1 &amp; 2 data with a U-Net + LSTM, more features (i.e. bands) and higher resolution produced better results (article, no code)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jremillard/images-to-osm">Find sports fields using Mask R-CNN and overlay on open-street-map</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/nasaharvest/togo-crop-mask">An LSTM to generate a crop mask for Togo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/michaeltrs/DeepSatModels">DeepSatModels</a> -&gt; Context-self contrastive pretraining for crop type semantic segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/simongrest/farm-pin-crop-detection-challenge">farm-pin-crop-detection-challenge</a> -&gt; Using eo-learn and fastai to identify crops from multi-spectral remote sensing data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/radiant-earth-insights/detecting-agricultural-croplands-from-sentinel-2-satellite-imagery-a025735d3bd8" rel="nofollow">Detecting Agricultural Croplands from Sentinel-2 Satellite Imagery</a> -&gt; We developed UNet-Agri, a benchmark machine learning model that classifies croplands using open-access Sentinel-2 imagery at 10m spatial resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/weecology/DeepTreeAttention">DeepTreeAttention</a> -&gt; Implementation of Hang et al. 2020 "Hyperspectral Image Classification with Attention Aided CNNs" for tree species prediction</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/nasaharvest/crop-mask">crop-mask</a> -&gt; End-to-end workflow for generating high resolution cropland maps, uses GEE &amp; LSTM model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lab-IDEAS/DeepCropMapping">DeepCropMapping</a> -&gt; A multi-temporal deep learning approach with improved spatial generalizability for dynamic corn and soybean mapping, uses LSTM</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/segment-satellite-imagery-using-ndvi-and-rasterio-6dcae02a044b" rel="nofollow">Segment Canopy Cover and Soil using NDVI and Rasterio</a></p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/florianbeyer/RandomForest-Classification">RandomForest-Classification</a> -&gt; Multisensor data to derive peatland vegetation communities using a fixed-wing unmanned aerial vehicle</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/antoine-spahr/Cocoa_plantations_detection">Cocoa_plantations_detection</a> -&gt; Detecting cocoa plantation in Ivory Coast using Sentinel-2 remote sensing data using KNN, SVM, Random Forest and MLP</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/AgriRS/SummerCrop_Deeplearning">SummerCrop_Deeplearning</a> -&gt; A Transferable Learning Classification Model and Carbon Sequestration Estimation of Crops in Farmland Ecosystem</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://deepforest.readthedocs.io/en/latest/index.html" rel="nofollow">DeepForest</a> is a python package for training and predicting individual tree crowns from airborne RGB imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/cienciaydatos/ai-challenge-trees">Official repository for the "Identifying trees on satellite images" challenge from Omdena</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/A2Amir/Counting-Trees-using-Satellite-Images">Counting-Trees-using-Satellite-Images</a> -&gt; create an inventory of incoming and outgoing trees for an annual tree inspections, uses keras &amp; semantic segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.nature.com/articles/s41586-020-2824-5" rel="nofollow">2020 Nature paper - An unexpectedly large count of trees in the West African Sahara and Sahel</a> -&gt; tree detection framework based on U-Net &amp; tensorflow 2 with code <a href="https://github.com/ankitkariryaa/An-unexpectedly-large-count-of-trees-in-the-western-Sahara-and-Sahel/tree/v1.0.0">here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/AmirNiaraki/TreeDetection">TreeDetection</a> -&gt; A color-based classifier to detect the trees in google image data along with tree visual localization and crown size calculations via OpenCV</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hr8yhtzb/PTDM">PTDM</a> -&gt; Pomelo Tree Detection Method Based on Attention Mechanism and Cross-Layer Feature Fusion</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jonathanventura/urban-tree-detection">urban-tree-detection</a> -&gt; Individual Tree Detection in Large-Scale Urban Environments using High-Resolution Multispectral Imagery. <div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation - Water, coastlines &amp; floods</h3><a id="user-content-segmentation---water-coastlines--floods" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šåˆ†æ®µ - æ°´ã€æµ·å²¸çº¿å’Œæ´ªæ°´" href="#segmentation---water-coastlines--floods"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<li>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://sahilkhose.medium.com/paper-presentation-e9bd0f3fb0bf" rel="nofollow">Semi-Supervised Classification and Segmentation on High Resolution Aerial Images - Solving the FloodNet problem</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lichtphyz/Houston_flooding">Houston_flooding</a> -&gt; labeling each pixel as either flooded or not using data from Hurricane Harvey. Dataset consisted of pre and post flood images, and a ground truth floodwater mask was created using unsupervised clustering (with DBScan) of image pixels with human cluster verification/adjustment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spaceml-org/ml4floods">ml4floods</a> -&gt; An ecosystem of data, models and code pipelines to tackle flooding with ML</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/cloud-to-street/jumpstart-your-machine-learning-satellite-competition-submission-2443b40d0a5a" rel="nofollow">A comprehensive guide to getting started with the ETCI Flood Detection competition</a> -&gt; using Sentinel1 SAR &amp; pytorch</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sweetlhare/STAC-Overflow">1st place solution for STAC Overflow: Map Floodwater from Radar Imagery hosted by Microsoft AI for Earth</a> -&gt; combines Unet with Catboostclassifier, taking their maxima, not the average</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Servir-Mekong/hydra-floods">hydra-floods</a> -&gt; an open source Python application for downloading, processing, and delivering surface water maps derived from remote sensing data</p>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/redouanelg/EddyNet">EddyNet</a> -&gt; A Deep Neural Network For Pixel-Wise Classification of Oceanic Eddies</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/deleo-lab/schisto-vegetation">schisto-vegetation</a> -&gt; Deep Learning Segmentation of Satellite Imagery Identifies Aquatic Vegetation Associated with Snail Intermediate Hosts of Schistosomiasis in Senegal, Africa</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/amazon-science/earth-forecasting-transformer">Earthformer</a> -&gt; Exploring space-time transformers for earth system forecasting</p>
</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Datalab-FIT-CTU/weather4cast-2022">WeatherFusionNet</a> -&gt; Predicting Precipitation from Satellite Data. weather4cast-2022 1st place solution</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MarcCoru/marinedebrisdetector">marinedebrisdetector</a> -&gt; Large-scale Detection of Marine Debris in Coastal Areas with Sentinel-2</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation - Roads &amp; sidewalks</h3><a id="user-content-segmentation---roads--sidewalks" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šåˆ†æ®µ - é“è·¯å’Œäººè¡Œé“" href="#segmentation---roads--sidewalks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Extracting roads is challenging due to the occlusions caused by other objects and the complex traffic environment</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/road-detection-using-segmentation-models-and-albumentations-libraries-on-keras-d5434eaf73a8" rel="nofollow">Road detection using semantic segmentation and albumentations for data augmention</a> using the Massachusetts Roads Dataset, U-net &amp; Keras. With <a href="https://github.com/Diyago/ML-DL-scripts/tree/master/DEEP%20LEARNING/segmentation/Segmentation%20pipeline">code</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LucasBrazCappelo/ML_EPFL_Project_2">ML_EPFL_Project_2</a> -&gt; U-Net in Pytorch to perform semantic segmentation of roads on satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://vihan-tyagi.medium.com/semantic-segmentation-of-satellite-images-based-on-deep-learning-algorithms-ea5ec408ac53" rel="nofollow">Semantic Segmentation of roads</a> using  U-net Keras, OSM data, project summary article by student, no code</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SpaceNetChallenge/RoadDetector">Winning Solutions from SpaceNet Road Detection and Routing Challenge</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gismodelling/RoadVecNet">RoadVecNet</a> -&gt; Road-Network-Segmentation-and-Vectorization in keras with dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/taspinar/sidl/blob/master/notebooks/2_Detecting_road_and_roadtypes_in_sattelite_images.ipynb">Detecting road and road types jupyter notebook</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/antran89/awesome-deep-map">awesome-deep-map</a> -&gt; A curated list of resources dedicated to deep learning / computer vision algorithms for mapping. The mapping problems include road network inference, building footprint extraction, etc.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mitroadmaps/roadtracer">RoadTracer: Automatic Extraction of Road Networks from Aerial Images</a> -&gt; uses an iterative search process guided by a CNN-based decision function to derive the road network graph directly from the output of the CNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ntelo007/road_detection_mtl">road_detection_mtl</a> -&gt; Road Detection using a multi-task Learning technique to improve the performance of the road detection task by incorporating prior knowledge constraints, uses the SpaceNet Roads Dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/anilbatra2185/road_connectivity">road_connectivity</a> -&gt; Improved Road Connectivity by Joint Learning of Orientation and Segmentation (CVPR2019)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/abhaykes1/Road-Network-Extraction">Road-Network-Extraction using classical Image processing</a> -&gt; blur &amp; canny edge detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wgcban/SPIN_RoadMapper">SPIN_RoadMapper</a> -&gt; Extracting Roads from Aerial Images via Spatial and Interaction Space Graph Reasoning for Autonomous Driving</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jiankang1991/road_extraction_remote_sensing">road_extraction_remote_sensing</a> -&gt; pytorch implementation, CVPR2018 DeepGlobe Road Extraction Challenge submission. See also <a href="https://github.com/zlckanata/DeepGlobe-Road-Extraction-Challenge">DeepGlobe-Road-Extraction-Challenge</a></p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mj129/CoANet">CoANet</a> -&gt; Connectivity Attention Network for Road Extraction From Satellite Imagery. The CoA module incorporates graphical information to ensure the connectivity of roads are better preserved</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/@nithishmailme/satellite-imagery-road-segmentation-ad2964dc3812" rel="nofollow">Satellite Imagery Road Segmentation</a> -&gt; intro articule on Medium using the kaggle <a href="https://www.kaggle.com/datasets/balraj98/massachusetts-roads-dataset" rel="nofollow">Massachusetts Roads Dataset</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/venkanna37/Label-Pixels">Label-Pixels</a> -&gt; for semantic segmentation of roads and other features</p>

</li>
<li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tist0bsc/SGCN">SGCN</a> -&gt; Split Depth-Wise Separable Graph-Convolution Network for Road Extraction in Complex Environments From High-Resolution Remote-Sensing Images</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation - Buildings &amp; rooftops</h3><a id="user-content-segmentation---buildings--rooftops" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šåˆ†å‰² - å»ºç­‘ç‰©å’Œå±‹é¡¶" href="#segmentation---buildings--rooftops"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Paulymorphous/Road-Segmentation">Road and Building Semantic Segmentation in Satellite Imagery</a> uses U-Net on the Massachusetts Roads Dataset &amp; keras</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/towards-artificial-intelligence/find-unauthorized-constructions-using-aerial-photography-and-deep-learning-with-code-part-2-b56ca80c8c99" rel="nofollow">find unauthorized constructions using aerial photography</a> -&gt; <a href="https://pub.towardsai.net/find-unauthorized-constructions-using-aerial-photography-and-deep-learning-with-code-part-1-6d3ca7ff6fa0" rel="nofollow">Dataset creation</a></p>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rodekruis/automated-building-detection">automated-building-detection</a> -&gt; Input: very-high-resolution (&lt;= 0.5 m/pixel) RGB satellite images. Output: buildings in vector format (geojson), to be used in digital map products. Built on top of robosat and robosat.pink.</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/AKASH2907/project_sunroof_india">project_sunroof_india</a> -&gt; Analyzed Google Satellite images to generate a report on individual house rooftop's solar power potential, uses a range of classical computer vision techniques (e.g Canny Edge Detection) to segment the roofs</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Segmentation - Solar panels</h3><a id="user-content-segmentation---solar-panels" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç»†åˆ† - å¤ªé˜³èƒ½ç”µæ± æ¿" href="#segmentation---solar-panels"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wangzhecheng/DeepSolar">DeepSolar</a> -&gt; A Machine Learning Framework to Efficiently Construct a Solar Deployment Database in the United States. <a href="https://www.kaggle.com/tunguz/deep-solar-dataset" rel="nofollow">Dataset on kaggle</a>, actually used a CNN for classification and segmentation is obtained by applying a threshold to the activation map. Original code is tf1 but <a href="https://github.com/aidan-fitz/deepsolar-v2">tf2/kers</a> and a <a href="https://github.com/wangzhecheng/deepsolar_pytorch">pytorch implementation</a> are available. Also checkout <a href="https://github.com/bessammehenni/DeepSolar_adoption_Virginia">Visualizations and in-depth analysis .. of the factors that can explain the adoption of solar energy in ..  Virginia</a> and <a href="https://github.com/gabrielkasmi/dsfrance">DeepSolar tracker: towards unsupervised assessment with open-source data of the accuracy of deep learning-based distributed PV mapping</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/fvergaracontesse/hyperion_solar_net">hyperion_solar_net</a> -&gt; trained classificaton &amp; segmentation models on RGB imagery from Google Maps</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kdmayer/3D-PV-Locator">3D-PV-Locator</a> -&gt; Large-scale detection of rooftop-mounted photovoltaic systems in 3D</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kdmayer/PV_Pipeline">PV_Pipeline</a> -&gt; DeepSolar for Germany</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dbaofd/solar-panels-detection">solar-panels-detection</a> -&gt; using SegNet, Fast SCNN &amp; ResNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/openclimatefix/predict_pv_yield">predict_pv_yield</a> -&gt; Using optical flow &amp; machine learning to predict PV yield</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/osmarluiz/Large-scale-solar-plant-monitoring">Large-scale-solar-plant-monitoring</a> -&gt; Remote Sensing for Monitoring of Photovoltaic Power Plants in Brazil Using Deep Semantic Segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/NREL/Panel-Segmentation">Panel-Segmentation</a> -&gt; Determine the presence of a solar array in the satellite image (boolean True/False), using a VGG16 classification model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ualsg/Roofpedia">Roofpedia</a> -&gt; an open registry of green roofs and solar roofs across the globe identified by Roofpedia through deep learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/nam-r/predicting-the-solar-potential-of-rooftops-using-image-segmentation-and-structured-data-61198c39d57c" rel="nofollow">Predicting the Solar Potential of Rooftops using Image Segmentation and Structured Data</a> Medium article, using 20cm imagery &amp; Unet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lkruitwagen/solar-pv-global-inventory">solar-pv-global-inventory</a></p>
</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lkruitwagen/remote-sensing-solar-pv">remote-sensing-solar-pv</a> -&gt; A repository for sharing progress on the automated detection of solar PV arrays in sentinel-2 remote sensing imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gabrieltseng/solar-panel-segmentation">solar-panel-segmentation)</a> -&gt; Finding solar panels using USGS satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tcapelle/solar_seg">solar_seg</a> -&gt; Solar segmentation of PV modules (sub elements of panels) using drone images and fast.ai</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Amirmoradi94/solar_plant_detection">solar_plant_detection</a> -&gt; boundary extraction of Photovoltaic (PV) plants using Mask RCNN and Amir dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/A-Stangeland/SolarDetection">SolarDetection</a> -&gt; unet on satellite image from the USA and France</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/francois-rozet/adopptrs">adopptrs</a> -&gt; Automatic Detection Of Photovoltaic Panels Through Remote Sensing using unet &amp; pytorch</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/TorrBorr/solar-panel-locator">solar-panel-locator</a> -&gt; the number of solar panel pixels was only ~0.2% of the total pixels in the dataset, so solar panel data was upsampled to account for the class imbalance</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/top-on/projects-solar-panel-detection">projects-solar-panel-detection</a> -&gt; List of project to detect solar panels from aerial/satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mjevans26/Satellite_ComputerVision">Satellite_ComputerVision</a> -&gt; UNET to detect solar arrays from Sentinel-2 data, using Google Earth Engine and Tensorflow. Also covers parking lot detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/riccardocadei/photovoltaic-detection">photovoltaic-detection</a> -&gt; Detecting available rooftop area from satellite images to install photovoltaic panels</p>

<li>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Instance segmentation</h2><a id="user-content-instance-segmentation" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå®ä¾‹åˆ†å‰²" href="#instance-segmentation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">In instance segmentation, each individual 'instance' of a segmented area is given a unique lable. For detection of very small objects this may a good approach, but it can struggle seperating individual objects that are closely spaced.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/matterport/Mask_RCNN">Mask_RCNN</a> generates bounding boxes and segmentation masks for each instance of an object in the image. It is very commonly used for instance segmentation &amp; object detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/saraivaufc/instance-segmentation-maskrcnn">Instance segmentation of center pivot irrigation system in Brazil</a> using free Landsat images, mask R-CNN &amp; Keras</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Mstfakts/Building-Detection-MaskRCNN">Building-Detection-MaskRCNN</a> -&gt; Building detection from the SpaceNet dataset by using Mask RCNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/georgiosouzounis/instance-segmentation-mask-rcnn">Oil tank instance segmentation with Mask R-CNN</a> with <a href="https://medium.com/@georgios.ouzounis/oil-storage-tank-instance-segmentation-with-mask-r-cnn-77c94433045f" rel="nofollow">accompanying article</a> using Keras &amp; Airbus Oil Storage Detection Dataset on Kaggle</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/OrdnanceSurvey/Mask_RCNN-for-Caravans">Mask_RCNN-for-Caravans</a> -&gt; detect caravan footprints from OS imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spiyer99/parking_bays_detectron2">parking_bays_detectron2</a> -&gt; Detecting parking bays with satellite imagery. Used Detectron2 and synthetic data with Unreal, superior performance to using Mask RCNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/my-rooftop-project-a-satellite-imagery-computer-vision-example-e45a296129a0" rel="nofollow">Locate buildings with a dark roof that feed heat island phenomenon using Mask RCNN</a> -&gt; with <a href="https://github.com/vintel38/RoofTop-Project">repo</a>, used INRIA dataset &amp; labelme for annotation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zinsmatt/Circle_Finder">Circle_Finder</a> -&gt; Circular Shapes Detection in Satellite Imagery, 2nd place solution to the Circle Finder Challenge</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/matthewnaples/Lawn_maskRCNN">Lawn_maskRCNN</a> -&gt; Detecting lawns from satellite images of properties in the Cedar Rapids area using Mask-R-CNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ecohydro/CropMask_RCNN">CropMask_RCNN</a> -&gt; Segmenting center pivot agriculture to monitor crop water use in drylands with Mask R-CNN and Landsat satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ashnair1/Mask-RCNN-for-Off-Nadir-Building-Detection">Mask RCNN for Spacenet Off Nadir Building Detection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yeliudev/CATNet">CATNet</a> -&gt; Learning to Aggregate Multi-Scale Context for Instance Segmentation in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ThayN15/Object-Detection-on-Satellite-Images-using-Mask-R-CNN">Object-Detection-on-Satellite-Images-using-Mask-R-CNN</a> -&gt; detect ships</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Junjue-Wang/FactSeg">FactSeg</a> -&gt; Foreground Activation Driven Small Object Semantic Segmentation in Large-Scale Remote Sensing Imagery (TGRS), also see <a href="https://github.com/Z-Zheng/FarSeg">FarSeg</a> and <a href="https://github.com/Z-Zheng/FreeNet">FreeNet</a>, implementations of research paper</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tclavelle/aqua_python">aqua_python</a> -&gt; detecting aquaculture farms using Mask R-CNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/KyanChen/RSPrompter">RSPrompter</a> -&gt; Learning to Prompt for Remote Sensing Instance Segmentation based on Visual Foundation Model</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection</h2><a id="user-content-object-detection" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹" href="#object-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/object-detection.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/object-detection.png" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Image showing the suitability of rotated bounding boxes in remote sensing.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Object detection in remote sensing involves locating and surrounding objects of interest with bounding boxes. Due to the large size of remote sensing images and the fact that objects may only comprise a few pixels, object detection can be challenging in this context. The imbalance between the area of the objects to be detected and the background, combined with the potential for objects to be easily confused with random features in the background, further complicates the task. Object detection generally performs better on larger objects, but becomes increasingly difficult as the objects become smaller and more densely packed. The accuracy of object detection models can also degrade rapidly as image resolution decreases, which is why it is common to use high resolution imagery, such as 30cm RGB, for object detection in remote sensing. A unique characteristic of aerial images is that objects can be oriented in any direction. To effectively extract measurements of the length and width of an object, it can be crucial to use rotated bounding boxes that align with the orientation of the object. This approach enables more accurate and meaningful analysis of the objects within the image. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/13/21/4291" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object tracking in videos</h3><a id="user-content-object-tracking-in-videos" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè§†é¢‘ä¸­çš„å¯¹è±¡è·Ÿè¸ª" href="#object-tracking-in-videos"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/vision4robotics/TCTrack">TCTrack</a> -&gt; Temporal Contexts for Aerial Tracking</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SY-Xuan/CFME">CFME</a> -&gt; Object Tracking in Satellite Videos by Improved Correlation Filters With Motion Estimations</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HeQibin/TGraM">TGraM</a> -&gt; Multi-Object Tracking in Satellite Videos with Graph-Based Multi-Task Modeling</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhangjunpeng9354/satellite_video_mod_groundtruth">satellite_video_mod_groundtruth</a> -&gt; groundtruth on satellite video for evaluating moving object detection algorithm</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ChaoXiao12/Moving-object-detection-DSFNet">Moving-object-detection-DSFNet</a> -&gt; DSFNet: Dynamic and Static Fusion Network for Moving Object Detection in Satellite Videos</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection with rotated bounding boxes</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection-with-rotated-bounding-boxes" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šä½¿ç”¨æ—‹è½¬è¾¹ç•Œæ¡†è¿›è¡Œå¯¹è±¡æ£€æµ‹" href="#object-detection-with-rotated-bounding-boxes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Orinted bounding boxes (OBB) are polygons representing rotated rectangles. For datasets checkout DOTA &amp; HRSC2016. Start with Yolov8</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/open-mmlab/mmrotate">mmrotate</a> -&gt; Rotated Object Detection Benchmark, with pretrained models and function for inferencing on very large images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jbwang1997/OBBDetection">OBBDetection</a> -&gt; an oriented object detection library, which is based on MMdetection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ming71/rotate-yolov3">rotate-yolov3</a> -&gt; Rotation object detection implemented with yolov3. Also see <a href="https://github.com/ming71/yolov3-polygon">yolov3-polygon</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liulei01/DRBox">DRBox</a> -&gt; for detection tasks where the objects are orientated arbitrarily, e.g. vehicles, ships and airplanes</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/csuhan/s2anet">s2anet</a> -&gt; Align Deep Features for Oriented Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ming71/CFC-Net">CFC-Net</a> -&gt; A Critical Feature Capturing Network for Arbitrary-Oriented Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/csuhan/ReDet">ReDet</a> -&gt; A Rotation-equivariant Detector for Aerial Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yijingru/BBAVectors-Oriented-Object-Detection">BBAVectors-Oriented-Object-Detection</a> -&gt; Oriented Object Detection in Aerial Images with Box Boundary-Aware Vectors</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Thinklab-SJTU/CSL_RetinaNet_Tensorflow">CSL_RetinaNet_Tensorflow</a> -&gt; Arbitrary-Oriented Object Detection with Circular Smooth Label</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SJTU-Thinklab-Det/r3det-on-mmdetection">r3det-on-mmdetection</a> -&gt; R3Det: Refined Single-Stage Detector with Feature Refinement for Rotating Object</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yangxue0827/R-DFPN_FPN_Tensorflow">R-DFPN_FPN_Tensorflow</a> -&gt; Rotation Dense Feature Pyramid Networks (Tensorflow)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/DetectionTeamUCAS/R2CNN_Faster-RCNN_Tensorflow">R2CNN_Faster-RCNN_Tensorflow</a> -&gt; Rotational region detection based on Faster-RCNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ming71/Rotated-RetinaNet">Rotated-RetinaNet</a> -&gt; implemented in pytorch, it supports the following datasets: DOTA, HRSC2016, ICDAR2013, ICDAR2015, UCAS-AOD, NWPU VHR-10, VOC2007</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ming71/OBBDet_Swin">OBBDet_Swin</a> -&gt; The sixth place winning solution in 2021 Gaofen Challenge</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WeiZongqi/CG-Net">CG-Net</a> -&gt; Learning Calibrated-Guidance for Object Detection in Aerial Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hukaixuan19970627/OrientedRepPoints_DOTA">OrientedRepPoints_DOTA</a> -&gt; Oriented RepPoints + Swin Transformer/ReResNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hukaixuan19970627/yolov5_obb">yolov5_obb</a> -&gt; yolov5 + Oriented Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://blog.roboflow.com/yolov5-for-oriented-object-detection/" rel="nofollow">How to Train YOLOv5 OBB</a> -&gt; YOLOv5 OBB tutorial and <a href="https://colab.research.google.com/drive/16nRwsioEYqWFLBF5VpT_NvELeOeupURM#scrollTo=1NZxhXTMWvek" rel="nofollow">YOLOv5 OBB noteboook</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SJTU-Thinklab-Det/OHDet_Tensorflow">OHDet_Tensorflow</a> -&gt; can be applied to rotation detection and object heading detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/nijkah/Seodore">Seodore</a> -&gt; framework maintaining recent updates of mmdetection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HsLOL/Rotation-RetinaNet-PyTorch">Rotation-RetinaNet-PyTorch</a> -&gt; oriented detector Rotation-RetinaNet implementation on Optical and SAR ship dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jwwangchn/aidet">AIDet</a> -&gt; an open source object detection in aerial image toolbox based on MMDetection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BossZard/rotation-yolov5">rotation-yolov5</a> -&gt; rotation detection based on yolov5</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lilinhao/ShipDetection">ShipDetection</a> -&gt; Ship Detection in HR Optical Remote Sensing Images via Rotated Bounding Box, based on Faster R-CNN and ORN, uses caffe</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LUCKMOONLIGHT/SLRDet">SLRDet</a> -&gt; project based on mmdetection to reimplement RRPN and use the model Faster R-CNN OBB</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RSIA-LIESMARS-WHU/AxisLearning">AxisLearning</a> -&gt; Axis Learning for Orientated Objects Detection in Aerial Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/whywhs/Detection_and_Recognition_in_Remote_Sensing_Image">Detection_and_Recognition_in_Remote_Sensing_Image</a> -&gt; This work uses PaNet to realize Detection and Recognition in Remote Sensing Image by MXNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZongxuPan/DrBox-v2-tensorflow">DrBox-v2-tensorflow</a> -&gt; tensorflow implementation of DrBox-v2 which is an improved detector with rotatable boxes for target detection in remote sensing images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HsLOL/Rotation-EfficientDet-D0">Rotation-EfficientDet-D0</a> -&gt; A PyTorch Implementation Rotation Detector based EfficientDet Detector, applied to custom rotation vehicle datasets</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yanqingyao1994/DODet">DODet</a> -&gt; Dual alignment for oriented object detection, uses DOTA dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WangJian981002/GF-CSL">GF-CSL</a> -&gt; Gaussian Focal Loss: Learning Distribution Polarized Angle Prediction for Rotated Object Detection in Aerial Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SIAnalytics/simplified_rbox_cnn">simplified_rbox_cnn</a> -&gt; RBox-CNN: rotated bounding box based CNN for ship detection in remote sensing image. Uses Tensorflow object detection API</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/flyingshan/Learning-Polar-Encodings-For-Arbitrary-Oriented-Ship-Detection-In-SAR-Images">Polar-Encodings</a> -&gt; Learning Polar Encodings for Arbitrary-Oriented Ship Detection in SAR Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZeroE04/R-CenterNet">R-CenterNet</a> -&gt; detector for rotated-object based on CenterNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/clobotics/piou">piou</a> -&gt; Orientated Object Detection; IoU Loss, applied to DOTA dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/steven-lang/DAFNe">DAFNe</a> -&gt; A One-Stage Anchor-Free Approach for Oriented Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/geovsion/AProNet">AProNet</a> -&gt; Detecting objects with precise orientation from aerial images. Applied to datasets DOTA and HRSC2016</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ming71/UCAS-AOD-benchmark">UCAS-AOD-benchmark</a> -&gt; A benchmark of UCAS-AOD dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/XinzeLee/RotateObjectDetection">RotateObjectDetection</a> -&gt; based on Ultralytics/yolov5, with adjustments to enable rotate prediction boxes. Also see <a href="https://github.com/XinzeLee/PolygonObjectDetection">PolygonObjectDetection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liuyanyi/AD-Toolbox">AD-Toolbox</a> -&gt; Aerial Detection Toolbox based on MMDetection and MMRotate, with support for more datasets</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Shank2358/GGHL">GGHL</a> -&gt; A General Gaussian Heatmap Label Assignment for Arbitrary-Oriented Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Shank2358/NPMMR-Det">NPMMR-Det</a> -&gt; A Novel Nonlocal-Aware Pyramid and Multiscale Multitask Refinement Detector for Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jbwang1997/AOPG">AOPG</a> -&gt; Anchor-Free Oriented Proposal Generator for Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Virusxxxxxxx/SE2-Det">SE2-Det</a> -&gt; Semantic-Edge-Supervised Single-Stage Detector for Oriented Object Detection in Remote Sensing Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LiWentomng/OrientedRepPoints">OrientedRepPoints</a> -&gt; Oriented RepPoints for Aerial Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Shank2358/TS-Conv">TS-Conv</a> -&gt; Task-wise Sampling Convolutions for Arbitrary-Oriented Object Detection in Aerial Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lzh420202/FCOSR">FCOSR</a> -&gt; A Simple Anchor-free Rotated Detector for Aerial Object Detection. This implement is modified from mmdetection. See also <a href="https://github.com/lzh420202/TensorRT_Inference">TensorRT_Inference</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HsLOL/OBB_Detection">OBB_Detection</a> -&gt; Finalist's solution in the track of Oriented Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images, 2022 Guangdong-Hong Kong-Macao Greater Bay Area International Algorithm Competition</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Li-Qingyun/sam-mmrotate">sam-mmrotate</a> -&gt; SAM (Segment Anything Model) for generating rotated bounding boxes with MMRotate, which is a comparison method of H2RBox-v2</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Chasel-Tsui/mmrotate-dcfl">mmrotate-dcfl</a> -&gt; Dynamic Coarse-to-Fine Learning for Oriented Tiny Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yangxue0827/h2rbox-mmrotate">h2rbox-mmrotate</a> -&gt; Horizontal Box Annotation is All You Need for Oriented Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yuhongtian17/Spatial-Transform-Decoupling">Spatial-Transform-Decoupling</a> -&gt; Spatial Transform Decoupling for Oriented Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/httle/ARS-DETR">ARS-DETR</a> -&gt; Aspect Ratio Sensitive Oriented Object Detection with Transformer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/shaunyuan22/CFINet">CFINet</a> -&gt; Small Object Detection via Coarse-to-fine Proposal Generation and Imitation Learning. Introduces <a href="https://shaunyuan22.github.io/SODA/" rel="nofollow">SODA-A dataset</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection enhanced by super resolution</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection-enhanced-by-super-resolution" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè¶…åˆ†è¾¨ç‡å¢å¼ºäº†ç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹" href="#object-detection-enhanced-by-super-resolution"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/super-resolution-and-object-detection-a-love-story-part-4-8ad971eef81e" rel="nofollow">Super-Resolution and Object Detection</a> -&gt; Super-resolution is a relatively inexpensive enhancement that can improve object detection performance</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Jakaria08/EESRGAN">EESRGAN</a> -&gt; Small-Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images with End-to-End Edge-Enhanced GAN and Object Detector Network</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.preprints.org/manuscript/202108.0337/v1" rel="nofollow">Mid-Low Resolution Remote Sensing Ship Detection Using Super-Resolved Feature Representation</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/divyam96/EESRGAN">EESRGAN</a> -&gt; Small-Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images with End-to-End Edge-Enhanced GAN and Object Detector Network. Applied to COWC &amp; <a href="https://data.mendeley.com/datasets/bkxj8z84m9/3" rel="nofollow">OGST</a> datasets</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wdzhao123/FBNet">FBNet</a> -&gt; Feature Balance for Fine-Grained Object Classification in Aerial Images</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/icey-zhang/SuperYOLO">SuperYOLO</a> -&gt; SuperYOLO: Super Resolution Assisted Object Detection in Multimodal Remote Sensing Imagery</p>

</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Salient object detection</h3><a id="user-content-salient-object-detection" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šæ˜¾ç€ç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹" href="#salient-object-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Detecting the most noticeable or important object in a scene</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MathLee/ACCoNet">ACCoNet</a> -&gt; Adjacent Context Coordination Network for Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MathLee/MCCNet">MCCNet</a> -&gt; Multi-Content Complementation Network for Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MathLee/CorrNet">CorrNet</a> -&gt; Lightweight Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images via Feature Correlation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MathLee/ORSI-SOD_Summary">Reading list for deep learning based Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rmcong/ORSSD-dataset">ORSSD-dataset</a> -&gt; salient object detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rmcong/EORSSD-dataset">EORSSD-dataset</a> -&gt; Extended Optical Remote Sensing Saliency Detection (EORSSD) Dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rmcong/DAFNet_TIP20">DAFNet_TIP20</a> -&gt; Dense Attention Fluid Network for Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Kunye-Shen/EMFINet">EMFINet</a> -&gt; Edge-Aware Multiscale Feature Integration Network for Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zxforchid/ERPNet">ERPNet</a> -&gt; Edge-guided Recurrent Positioning Network for Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zxforchid/FSMINet">FSMINet</a> -&gt; Fully Squeezed Multi-Scale Inference Network for Fast and Accurate Saliency Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/NuaaYH/AGNet">AGNet</a> -&gt; AGNet: Attention Guided Network for Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/NuaaYH/MSCNet">MSCNet</a> -&gt; A lightweight multi-scale context network for salient object detection in optical remote sensing images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liuyu1002/GPnet">GPnet</a> -&gt; Global Perception Network for Salient Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MathLee/SeaNet">SeaNet</a> -&gt; Lightweight Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images via Semantic Matching and Edge Alignment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MathLee/GeleNet">GeleNet</a> -&gt; Salient Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images Driven by Transformer</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Buildings, rooftops &amp; solar panels</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---buildings-rooftops--solar-panels" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹ - å»ºç­‘ç‰©ã€å±‹é¡¶å’Œå¤ªé˜³èƒ½ç”µæ± æ¿" href="#object-detection---buildings-rooftops--solar-panels"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yasserius/satellite_image_tinhouse_detector">satellite_image_tinhouse_detector</a> -&gt; Detection of tin houses from satellite/aerial images using the Tensorflow Object Detection API</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://omdena.com/blog/machine-learning-rooftops/" rel="nofollow">Machine Learning For Rooftop Detection and Solar Panel Installment</a> discusses tiling large images and generating annotations from OSM data. Features of the roofs were calculated using a combination of contour detection and classification. <a href="https://omdena.com/blog/rooftops-classification/" rel="nofollow">Follow up article using semantic segmentation</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/building-extraction-with-yolt2-and-spacenet-data-a926f9ffac4f" rel="nofollow">Building Extraction with YOLT2 and SpaceNet Data</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dbuscombe-usgs/XBD-hurricanes">XBD-hurricanes</a> -&gt; Models for building (and building damage) detection in high-resolution (&lt;1m) satellite and aerial imagery using a modified RetinaNet model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/weekend-project-detecting-solar-panels-from-satellite-imagery-f6f5d5e0da40" rel="nofollow">Detecting solar panels from satellite imagery</a> using segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/aurotripathy/ssd-spacenet">ssd-spacenet</a> -&gt; Detect buildings in the Spacenet dataset using Single Shot MultiBox Detector (SSD)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LllC-mmd/3DBuildingInfoMap">3DBuildingInfoMap</a> -&gt; simultaneous extraction of building height and footprint from Sentinel imagery using ResNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/analytics-vidhya/solar-panel-detection-from-aerial-view-or-satellite-images-648c22c260ba" rel="nofollow">Solar Panel Detection</a> -&gt; using Faster R-CNN &amp; Tensorflow object detection API. With <a href="https://github.com/shiva2410/Solar_Panel-Detection-in-Aerial-Images">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/thinkpractice/DeepSolaris">DeepSolaris</a> -&gt; a EuroStat project to detect solar panels in aerial images, further material <a href="https://github.com/FHNW-IVGI/workshop_geopython2019/tree/master/Ex.02_SolarPanels">here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Qberto/ML_ObjectDetection_CAFO">ML_ObjectDetection_CAFO</a> -&gt; Detect Concentrated Animal Feeding Operations (CAFO) in Satellite Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/luoxiaoliaolan/Multi-level-Building-Detection-Framework">Multi-level-Building-Detection-Framework</a> -&gt; Multilevel Building Detection Framework in Remote Sensing Images Based on Convolutional Neural Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://dds-lab.github.io/disaster-damage-detection/" rel="nofollow">Automatic Damage Annotation on Post-Hurricane Satellite Imagery</a> -&gt; detect damaged buildings using tensorflow object detection API. With repos <a href="https://github.com/DDS-Lab/disaster-image-processing">here</a> and <a href="https://github.com/annieyan/PreprocessSatelliteImagery-ObjectDetection">here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/krishanr/mappingchallenge">mappingchallenge</a> -&gt; YOLOv5 applied to the AICrowd Mapping Challenge dataset</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Ships &amp; boats</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---ships--boats" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹ - èˆ¹èˆ¶" href="#object-detection---ships--boats"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/robmarkcole/kaggle-ships-in-Google-Earth-yolov5">kaggle-ships-in-Google-Earth-yolov5</a> -&gt; Applying YOLOv5 to Kaggle Ships in Google Earth dataset</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/earthcube-stories/how-hard-it-is-for-an-ai-to-detect-ships-on-satellite-images-7265e34aadf0" rel="nofollow">How hard is it for an AI to detect ships on satellite images?</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/object-detection-in-satellite-imagery-a-low-overhead-approach-part-i-cbd96154a1b7" rel="nofollow">Object Detection in Satellite Imagery, a Low Overhead Approach</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/dataseries/detecting-ships-in-satellite-imagery-7f0ca04e7964" rel="nofollow">Detecting Ships in Satellite Imagery</a> using the Planet dataset and Keras</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/planetlabs/notebooks/blob/master/jupyter-notebooks/ship-detector/01_ship_detector.ipynb">Planet use non DL felzenszwalb algorithm to detect ships</a></p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/data-science-and-satellite-imagery-985229e1cd2f" rel="nofollow">Ship detection using k-means clustering &amp; CNN classifier on patches</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MJCruickshank/SARfish">SARfish</a> -&gt; Ship detection in Sentinel 1 Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JinleiMa/ASD">Arbitrary-Oriented Ship Detection through Center-Head Point Extraction</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rugg2/ship_detection">ship_detection</a> -&gt; using an interesting combination of CNN classifier, Class Activation Mapping (CAM) &amp; UNET segmentation. Accompanying <a href="https://www.vortexa.com/insights/technology/satellite-images-object-detection/" rel="nofollow">three part blog post</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/intel-software-innovators/ship-detection-in-satellite-images-from-scratch-849ccfcc3072" rel="nofollow">Building a complete Ship detection algorithm using YOLOv3 and Planet satellite images</a> -&gt; covers finding and annotating data (using LabelMe), preprocessing large images into chips, and training Yolov3. <a href="https://github.com/amanbasu/ship-detection">Repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zmf0507/Ship-detection-in-satellite-images">Ship-detection-in-satellite-images</a> -&gt; experiments with  UNET, YOLO, Mask R-CNN, SSD, Faster R-CNN, RETINA-NET</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/debasis-dotcom/Ship-Detection-from-Satellite-Images-using-YOLOV4">Ship-Detection-from-Satellite-Images-using-YOLOV4</a> -&gt; uses Kaggle Airbus Ship Detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/toshi-k/kaggle-airbus-ship-detection-challenge">kaggle-airbus-ship-detection-challenge</a> -&gt; using oriented SSD</p>
