<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rhammell/shipsnet-detector">shipsnet-detector</a> -&gt; Detect container ships in Planet imagery using machine learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/classifying-ships-in-satellite-imagery-with-neural-networks-944024879651" rel="nofollow">Classifying Ships in Satellite Imagery with Neural Networks</a> -&gt; applied to the Kaggle Ships in Satellite Imagery dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/@gabogarza/mask-r-cnn-for-ship-detection-segmentation-a1108b5a083" rel="nofollow">Mask R-CNN for Ship Detection &amp; Segmentation</a> blog post with <a href="https://github.com/gabrielgarza/Mask_RCNN">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/alina2204/contrastive_SSL_ship_detection">contrastive_SSL_ship_detection</a> -&gt; Contrastive self supervised learning for ship detection in Sentinel 2 images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/@ipmach/boat-detection-with-multi-region-growing-method-in-satellite-images-3339a6c29a8c" rel="nofollow">Boat detection with multi-region-growing method in satellite images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/swricci/small-boat-detector">small-boat-detector</a> -&gt; Trained yolo v3 model weights and configuration file to detect small boats in satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JasonManesis/Satellite-Imagery-Datasets-Containing-Ships">Satellite-Imagery-Datasets-Containing-Ships</a> -&gt; A list of optical and radar satellite datasets for ship detection, classification, semantic segmentation and instance segmentation tasks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/allenai/vessel-detection-sentinels">vessel-detection-sentinels</a> -&gt; Sentinel-1 and Sentinel-2 Vessel Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gouravbarkle/Ship-Detection">Ship-Detection</a> -&gt; CNN approach for ship detection in the ocean using a satellite image</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/carlossantamarizq/vesselTracker">vesselTracker</a> -&gt; Project based on reduced model of Yolov5 architecture using Pytorch. Custom dataset based on SAR imagery provided by Sentinel-1 through Earth Engine API</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/danieltyukov/marine-debris-ml-model">marine-debris-ml-model</a> -&gt; Marine Debris Detection using tensorflow object detection API</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WangZhenqing-RS/SDGH-Net-Ship-Detection-in-Optical-Remote-Sensing-Images-Based-on-Gaussian-Heatmap-Regression">SDGH-Net</a> -&gt; Ship Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images Based on Gaussian Heatmap Regression</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lausen-Ng/LR-TSDet">LR-TSDet</a> -&gt; LR-TSDet: Towards Tiny Ship Detection in Low-Resolution Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/DYH666/FGSCR-42">FGSCR-42</a> -&gt; A public Dataset for Fine-Grained Ship Classification in Remote sensing images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lilinhao/ShipDetection">ShipDetection</a> -&gt; Ship Detection in HR Optical Remote Sensing Images via Rotated Bounding Box, based on Faster R-CNN and ORN, uses caffe</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lilytopia/WakeNet">WakeNet</a> -&gt; Rethinking Automatic Ship Wake Detection: State-of-the-Art CNN-based Wake Detection via Optical Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/histogram-of-oriented-gradients-hog-heading-classification-a92d1cf5b3cc" rel="nofollow">Histogram of Oriented Gradients (HOG) Boat Heading Classification</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/object-detection-in-satellite-imagery-a-low-overhead-approach-part-i-cbd96154a1b7" rel="nofollow">Object Detection in Satellite Imagery, a Low Overhead Approach</a> -&gt; Medium article which demonstrates how to combine Canny edge detector pre-filters with HOG feature descriptors, random forest classifiers, and sliding windows to perform ship detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SIAnalytics/simplified_rbox_cnn">simplified_rbox_cnn</a> -&gt; RBox-CNN: rotated bounding box based CNN for ship detection in remote sensing image. Uses Tensorflow object detection API</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xlsjdjdk/Ship-Detection-based-on-YOLOv3-and-KV260">Ship-Detection-based-on-YOLOv3-and-KV260</a> -&gt; entry project of the Xilinx Adaptive Computing Challenge 2021. It uses YOLOv3 for ship target detection in optical remote sensing images, and deploys DPU on the KV260 platform to achieve hardware acceleration</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WindVChen/LEVIR-Ship">LEVIR-Ship</a> -&gt; a dataset for tiny ship detection under medium-resolution remote sensing images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WindVChen/Push-and-Pull-Network">Push-and-Pull-Network</a> -&gt; Contrastive Learning for Fine-grained Ship Classification in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WindVChen/DRENet">DRENet</a> -&gt; A Degraded Reconstruction Enhancement-Based Method for Tiny Ship Detection in Remote Sensing Images With a New Large-Scale Dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BloodAxe/xView3-The-First-Place-Solution">xView3-The-First-Place-Solution</a> -&gt; A winning solution for <a href="https://iuu.xview.us/" rel="nofollow">xView 3</a> challenge (Vessel detection, classification and length estimation on Sentinetl-1 images). Contains trained models, inference pipeline and training code &amp; configs to reproduce the results.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/allenai/vessel-detection-viirs">vessel-detection-viirs</a> -&gt; Model and service code for streaming vessel detections from VIIRS satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/iamyadavabhishek/anomaly-detection-in-SAR-imagery">anomaly-detection-in-SAR-imagery</a> -&gt; identify an unknown ship in docks using keras &amp; retinanet</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Cars, vehicles &amp; trains</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---cars-vehicles--trains" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹ - æ±½è½¦ã€è½¦è¾†å’Œç«è½¦" href="#object-detection---cars-vehicles--trains"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spiyer99/retinanet">Detection of parkinglots and driveways with retinanet</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MichelHalmes/pytorch-vedai">pytorch-vedai</a> -&gt; object detection on the VEDAI dataset: Vehicle Detection in Aerial Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hfisser/Truck_Detection_Sentinel2_COVID19">Truck Detection with Sentinel-2 during COVID-19 crisis</a> -&gt; moving objects in Sentinel-2 data causes a specific reflectance relationship in the RGB, which looks like a rainbow, and serves as a marker for trucks. Improve accuracy by only analysing roads. Not using object detection but relevant. Also see <a href="https://github.com/hfisser/S2TD">S2TD</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/motokimura/cowc_car_counting">cowc_car_counting</a> -&gt; car counting on the <a href="https://gdo152.llnl.gov/cowc/" rel="nofollow">Cars Overhead With Context (COWC) dataset</a>. Not sctictly object detection but a CNN to predict the car count in a tile</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JacksonPeoples/CarCounting">CarCounting</a> -&gt; using Yolov3 &amp; COWC dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://omdena.com/blog/ai-road-safety/" rel="nofollow">Traffic density estimation as a regression problem instead of object detection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://orbitalinsight.com/blog/apping-computer-vision-to-railcar-detection" rel="nofollow">Applying Computer Vision to Railcar Detection</a> -&gt; useful insights into counting railcars (i.e. train carriages) using Mask-RCNN with rotated bounding boxes output</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://orbitalinsight.com/blog/leveraging-deep-learning-for-vehicle-detection-and-classification" rel="nofollow">Leveraging Deep Learning for Vehicle Detection And Classification</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HsLOL/Rotation-EfficientDet-D0">Rotation-EfficientDet-D0</a> -&gt; PyTorch implementation of Rotated EfficientDet, applied to a custom rotation vehicle dataset (car counting)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/YinongGuo/RSVC2021-Dataset">RSVC2021-Dataset</a> -&gt; A dataset for Vehicle Counting in Remote Sensing images, created from the DOTA &amp; ITCVD</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/car-localization-and-counting-with-overhead-imagery-an-interactive-exploration-9d5a029a596b" rel="nofollow">Car Localization and Counting with Overhead Imagery, an Interactive Exploration</a> -&gt; Medium article by Adam Van Etten</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hbsszq/Vehicle-Counting-in-Very-Low-Resolution-Aerial-Images">Vehicle-Counting-in-Very-Low-Resolution-Aerial-Images</a> -&gt; Vehicle Counting in Very Low-Resolution Aerial Images via Cross-Resolution Spatial Consistency and Intraresolution Time Continuity</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.silvispace.xyz/posts/vehicle-post/" rel="nofollow">Vehicle Detection blog post</a> by Grant Pearse: detecting vehicles across New Zealand without collecting local training data</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Planes &amp; aircraft</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---planes--aircraft" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹ - é£æœºå’Œé£æœº" href="#object-detection---planes--aircraft"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ShubhankarRawat/Airplane-Detection-for-Satellites">Faster RCNN to detect airplanes</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/avanetten/yoltv4">yoltv4</a> includes examples on the <a href="https://registry.opendata.aws/rareplanes/" rel="nofollow">RarePlanes dataset</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hakeemtfrank/aircraft-detection">aircraft-detection</a> -&gt; experiments to test the performance of a Gaussian process (GP) classifier with various kernels on the UC Merced land use land cover (LULC) dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://share.buitrongan.com/using-detectron2-to-segments-aircraft-from-satellite-images-5a8ac1a0d35e" rel="nofollow">Using Detectron2 to segment aircraft from satellite imagery</a> -&gt; pytorch and Rare Planes</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/emrekrtorun/aircraft-detection-from-satellite-images-yolov3">aircraft-detection-from-satellite-images-yolov3</a> -&gt; trained on kaggle cgi-planes-in-satellite-imagery-w-bboxes dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dilsadunsal/HRPlanesv2-Data-Set">HRPlanesv2-Data-Set</a> -&gt; YOLOv4 and YOLOv5 weights trained on the HRPlanesv2 dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Shayan-Bravo/Deep-Learning-for-Aircraft-Recognition">Deep-Learning-for-Aircraft-Recognition</a> -&gt; A CNN model trained to classify and identify various military aircraft through satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Huatsing-Lau/FRCNN-for-Aircraft-Detection">FRCNN-for-Aircraft-Detection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/evilsocket/ergo-planes-detector">ergo-planes-detector</a> -&gt; An ergo based project that relies on a convolutional neural network to detect airplanes from satellite imagery, uses the PlanesNet dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/miko7879/pytorch-remote-sensing">pytorch-remote-sensing</a> -&gt; Aircraft detection using the 'Airbus Aircraft Detection' dataset and Faster-RCNN with ResNet-50 backbone using pytorch</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/UKMIITB/FasterRCNN_ObjectDetection">FasterRCNN_ObjectDetection</a> -&gt; faster RCNN model for aircraft detection and localisation in satellite images and creating a webpage with live server for public usage</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/TolgaBkm/HRPlanes">HRPlanes</a> -&gt; weights of YOLOv4 and Faster R-CNN networks trained with HRPlanes dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/alexbakr/aerial-detection">aerial-detection</a> -&gt; uses Yolov5 &amp; Icevision</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/artificialis/how-to-choose-a-deep-learning-model-to-detect-aircrafts-in-satellite-imagery-cd7d106e76ad" rel="nofollow">How to choose a deep learning architecture to detect aircrafts in satellite imagery?</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jeffaudi/rareplanes-yolov5">rareplanes-yolov5</a> -&gt; using YOLOv5 and the RarePlanes dataset to detect and classify sub-characteristics of aircraft, with <a href="https://medium.com/artificialis/detecting-aircrafts-on-airbus-pleiades-imagery-with-yolov5-5f3d464b75ad" rel="nofollow">article</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/naivelogic/OnlyPlanes">OnlyPlanes</a> -&gt; Incrementally Tuning Synthetic Training Datasets for Satellite Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://encord.com/blog/rareplane-dataset-aircraft-detection-model/" rel="nofollow">Understanding the RarePlanes Dataset and Building an Aircraft Detection Model</a> -&gt; blog post</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Infrastructure &amp; utilities</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---infrastructure--utilities" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¯¹è±¡æ£€æµ‹ - åŸºç¡€è®¾æ–½å’Œå…¬ç”¨äº‹ä¸š" href="#object-detection---infrastructure--utilities"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lbborkowski/wind-turbine-detector">wind-turbine-detector</a> -&gt; Wind Turbine Object Detection from Aerial Imagery Using TensorFlow Object Detection API</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/EduardoFernandes1410/PATREO-Dengue">Water Tanks and Swimming Pools Detection</a> -&gt; uses Faster R-CNN</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/13/7/1243" rel="nofollow">PCAN</a> -&gt; Part-Based Context Attention Network for Thermal Power Plant Detection in Remote Sensing Imagery, with <a href="https://github.com/wenxinYin/AIR-TPPDD">dataset</a></p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Oil storage tank detection</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---oil-storage-tank-detection" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹-å‚¨æ²¹ç½æ£€æµ‹" href="#object-detection---oil-storage-tank-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Oil is stored in tanks at many points between extraction and sale, and the volume of oil in storage is an important economic indicator.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/planet-stories/a-beginners-guide-to-calculating-oil-storage-tank-occupancy-with-help-of-satellite-imagery-e8f387200178" rel="nofollow">A Beginnerâ€™s Guide To Calculating Oil Storage Tank Occupancy With Help Of Satellite Imagery</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/oil-storage-tanks-volume-occupancy-on-satellite-imagery-using-yolov3-3cf251362d9d" rel="nofollow">Oil Storage Tankâ€™s Volume Occupancy On Satellite Imagery Using YoloV3</a> with <a href="https://github.com/mdmub0587/Oil-Storage-Tank-s-Volume-Occupancy">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kheyer/Oil-Tank-Volume-Estimation">Oil-Tank-Volume-Estimation</a> -&gt; combines object detection and classical computer vision</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/georgiosouzounis/instance-segmentation-mask-rcnn">Oil tank instance segmentation with Mask R-CNN</a> with <a href="https://medium.com/@georgios.ouzounis/oil-storage-tank-instance-segmentation-with-mask-r-cnn-77c94433045f" rel="nofollow">accompanying article</a> using Keras &amp; Airbus Oil Storage Detection Dataset on Kaggle</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/anttad/SubpixelCircleDetection">SubpixelCircleDetection</a> -&gt; CIRCULAR-SHAPED OBJECT DETECTION IN LOW RESOLUTION SATELLITE IMAGES</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/TheodorEmanuelsson/oil_storage-detector">oil_storage-detector</a> -&gt; using yolov5 and the Airbus Oil Storage Detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dzubke/oil_well_detector">oil_well_detector</a> -&gt; detect oil wells in the Bakken oil field based on satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/artificialis/oil-storage-detection-on-airbus-imagery-with-yolox-9e38eb6f7e62" rel="nofollow">Oil Storage Detection on Airbus Imagery with YOLOX</a> -&gt; uses the Kaggle Airbus Oil Storage Detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/anttad/AContrarioTankDetection">AContrarioTankDetection</a> -&gt; Oil Tank Detection in Satellite Images via a Contrario Clustering</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Animals</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---animals" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç‰©ä½“æ£€æµ‹ - åŠ¨ç‰©" href="#object-detection---animals"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">A variety of techniques can be used to count animals, including object detection and instance segmentation. For convenience they are all listed here:</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/IssamLaradji/cownter_strike">cownter_strike</a> -&gt; counting cows, located with point-annotations, two models: CSRNet (a density-based method) &amp; LCFCN (a detection-based method)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/akharina/elephant_detection">elephant_detection</a> -&gt; Using Keras-Retinanet to detect elephants from aerial images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sriramelango/CNN-Mosquito-Detection">CNN-Mosquito-Detection</a> -&gt; determining the locations of potentially dangerous breeding grounds, compared YOLOv4, YOLOR &amp; YOLOv5</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lynch-lab/Borowicz_etal_Spacewhale">Borowicz_etal_Spacewhale</a> -&gt; locate whales using ResNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sweetlhare/walrus-detection-and-count">walrus-detection-and-count</a> -&gt; uses Mask R-CNN instance segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Pangoraw/MarineMammalsDetection">MarineMammalsDetection</a> -&gt; Weakly Supervised Detection of Marine Animals in High Resolution Aerial Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RiceD2KLab/Audubon_F21">Audubon_F21</a> -&gt;  Deep object detection for waterbird monitoring using aerial imagery</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object detection - Miscellaneous</h3><a id="user-content-object-detection---miscellaneous" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¯¹è±¡æ£€æµ‹ - å…¶ä»–" href="#object-detection---miscellaneous"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/@ije_good/object-detection-on-satellite-imagery-using-retinanet-part-1-training-e589975afbd5" rel="nofollow">Object detection on Satellite Imagery using RetinaNet</a> -&gt; using the Kaggle Swimming Pool and Car Detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://blog.roboflow.com/tackling-the-small-object-problem-in-object-detection" rel="nofollow">Tackling the Small Object Problem in Object Detection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/12/10/1667" rel="nofollow">Object Detection and Image Segmentation with Deep Learning on Earth Observation Data: A Review</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/murari023/awesome-aerial-object-detection">awesome-aerial-object-detection bu murari023</a>, <a href="https://github.com/visionxiang/awesome-object-detection-in-aerial-images">another by visionxiang</a> and <a href="https://github.com/kuanhungchen/awesome-tiny-object-detection">awesome-tiny-object-detection</a> list many relevant papers</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/the-satellite-utility-manifold-object-detection-accuracy-as-a-function-of-image-resolution-ebb982310e8c" rel="nofollow">Object Detection Accuracy as a Function of Image Resolution</a> -&gt; Medium article using COWC dataset, performance rapidly degrades below 30cm imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/avanetten/simrdwn">Satellite Imagery Multiscale Rapid Detection with Windowed Networks (SIMRDWN)</a> -&gt; combines some of the leading object detection algorithms into a unified framework designed to detect objects both large and small in overhead imagery. Train models and test on arbitrary image sizes with YOLO (versions 2 and 3), Faster R-CNN, SSD, or R-FCN.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/avanetten/yoltv4">YOLTv4</a> -&gt; YOLTv4 is designed to detect objects in aerial or satellite imagery in arbitrarily large images that far exceed the ~600Ã—600 pixel size typically ingested by deep learning object detection frameworks. Read <a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/announcing-yoltv4-improved-satellite-imagery-object-detection-f5091e913fad" rel="nofollow">Announcing YOLTv4: Improved Satellite Imagery Object Detection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yangxue0827/RotationDetection">Tensorflow Benchmarks for Object Detection in Aerial Images</a></p>
</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dingjiansw101/AerialDetection">Pytorch Benchmarks for Object Detection in Aerial Images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liuqingjie/ASPDNet">ASPDNet</a> -&gt; Counting dense objects in remote sensing images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ultralytics/xview-yolov3">xview-yolov3</a> -&gt; xView 2018 Object Detection Challenge: YOLOv3 Training and Inference</p>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/asimniazi63/Object-Detection-on-Satellite-Images">Object Detection Satellite Imagery Multi-vehicles Dataset (SIMD)</a> -&gt; RetinaNet,Yolov3 and Faster RCNN for multi object detection on satellite images dataset</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/NASA-IMPACT/marine_debris_ML">marine_debris_ML</a> -&gt; Marine debris detection, uses 3-meter imagery product called Planetscope with bands in the red, green, blue, and near-infrared. Uses Tensorflow Object Detection API with pre-trained resnet 101</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/pool-detection-from-aerial-imagery-f5b76d0a6093" rel="nofollow">pool-detection-from-aerial-imagery</a> -&gt; Use Icevision and Detectron2 to detect swimming pools from aerial imagery</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/qsjxyz/Electric-Pylon-Detection-in-RSI">Electric-Pylon-Detection-in-RSI</a> -&gt; a dataset which contains 1500 remote sensing images of electric pylons used to train ten deep learning models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.iqt.org/synthesizing-robustness-yoltv4-results-part-2-dataset-size-requirements-and-geographic-insights/" rel="nofollow">Synthesizing Robustness YOLTv4 Results Part 2: Dataset Size Requirements and Geographic Insights</a> -&gt; quantify how much harder rare objects are to localize</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sustainlab-group/IS-Count">IS-Count</a> -&gt; IS-Count is a sampling-based and learnable method for estimating the total object count in a region</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/object-detection-on-aerial-imagery-using-retinanet-626130ba2203" rel="nofollow">Object Detection On Aerial Imagery Using RetinaNet</a></p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/fyangneil/Clustered-Object-Detection-in-Aerial-Image">Clustered-Object-Detection-in-Aerial-Image</a></p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/KevinMuyaoGuo/yolov5s_for_satellite_imagery">yolov5s_for_satellite_imagery</a> -&gt; yolov5s applied to the DOTA dataset</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HsLOL/RetinaNet-PyTorch">RetinaNet-PyTorch</a> -&gt; RetinaNet implementation on remote sensing ship dataset (SSDD)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ShubhayanS/Detecting-Cyclone-Centers-Custom-YOLOv3">Detecting-Cyclone-Centers-Custom-YOLOv3</a> -&gt; tropical cyclones (TCs) are intense warm-corded cyclonic vortices, developed from low-pressure systems over the tropical oceans and driven by complex air-sea interaction</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/bostankhan6/Object-Detection-YoloV3-RetinaNet-FasterRCNN">Object-Detection-YoloV3-RetinaNet-FasterRCNN</a> -&gt; trained on a private datset</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/InnovAIco/Google-earth-Object-Recognition">Google-earth-Object-Recognition</a> -&gt; Code for training and evaluating on Dior Dataset (Google Earth Images) using RetinaNet and YOLOV5</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/sentinel-hub/hiector-hierarchical-object-detector-at-scale-5a61753b51a3" rel="nofollow">HIECTOR: Hierarchical object detector at scale</a> -&gt; HIECTOR facilitates multiple satellite data collections of increasingly detailed spatial resolution for a cost-efficient and accurate object detection over large areas. <a href="https://github.com/sentinel-hub/hiector">Code</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WenchaoliuMUC/Detection-of-Multiclass-Objects-in-Optical-Remote-Sensing-Images">Detection of Multiclass Objects in Optical Remote Sensing Images</a> -&gt; Detection of Multiclass Objects in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/weihancug/Sampling-Balance_Multi-stage_Network">SB-MSN</a> -&gt; Improving Training Instance Quality in Aerial Image Object Detection With a Sampling-Balance-Based Multistage Network</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/avanetten/yoltv5">yoltv5</a> -&gt; detects objects in arbitrarily large aerial or satellite images that far exceed the ~600Ã—600 pixel size typically ingested by deep learning object detection frameworks. Uses YOLOv5 &amp; pytorch</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Accenture/AIR">AIR</a> -&gt; A deep learning object detector framework written in Python for supporting Land Search and Rescue Missions</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hm-better/dior_detect">dior_detect</a> -&gt; benchmarks for object detection on DIOR dataset</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/panchromatic-to-multispectral-object-detection-performance-as-a-function-of-imaging-bands-51ecaaa3dc56" rel="nofollow">Panchromatic to Multispectral: Object Detection Performance as a Function of Imaging Bands</a> -&gt; Medium article, concludes that more bands are not always beneficial, but likely varies by use case</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yf19970118/OPLD-Pytorch">OPLD-Pytorch</a> -&gt; Learning Point-Guided Localization for Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yxhnjust/F3Net">F3Net</a> -&gt; Feature Fusion and Filtration Network for Object Detection in Optical Remote Sensing Images</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Zhu1Teng/GLNet">GLNet</a> -&gt; Global to Local: Clip-LSTM-Based Object Detection From Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Complicateddd/SRAF-Net">SRAF-Net</a> -&gt; A Scene-Relevant Anchor-Free Object Detection Network in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/EEexplorer001/object_detection_in_remote_sensing_images">object_detection_in_remote_sensing_images</a> -&gt; using CNN and attention mechanism</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hiroki-kawauchi/SHAPObjectDetection">SHAPObjectDetection</a> -&gt; SHAP-Based Interpretable Object Detection Method for Satellite Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jwwangchn/NWD">NWD</a> -&gt; A Normalized Gaussian Wasserstein Distance for Tiny Object Detection. Uses AI-TOD dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZhAnGToNG1/MSFC-Net">MSFC-Net</a> -&gt; Multiscale Semantic Fusion-Guided Fractal Convolutional Object Detection Network for Optical Remote Sensing Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Shank2358/LO-Det">LO-Det</a> -&gt; LO-Det: Lightweight Oriented Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/shnew/R2IPoints">R2IPoints</a> -&gt;  Pursuing Rotation-Insensitive Point Representation for Aerial Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xiaojs18/Object-Detection">Object-Detection</a> -&gt; Multi-Scale Object Detection with the Pixel Attention Mechanism in a Complex Background</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Chasel-Tsui/mmdet-rfla">mmdet-rfla</a> -&gt; RFLA: Gaussian Receptive based Label Assignment for Tiny Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ChungYi347/Interactive-Multi-Class-Tiny-Object-Detection">Interactive-Multi-Class-Tiny-Object-Detection</a> -&gt; Interactive Multi-Class Tiny-Object Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/fcakyon/small-object-detection-benchmark">small-object-detection-benchmark</a> -&gt; Slicing Aided Hyper Inference and Fine-tuning for Small Object Detection (SAHI)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/muzairkhattak/OD-Satellite-iSAID">OD-Satellite-iSAID</a> -&gt; Object Detection in Aerial Images: A Case Study on Performance Improvement using iSAID</p>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Object counting</h2><a id="user-content-object-counting" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¯¹è±¡è®¡æ•°" href="#object-counting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">When the object count, but not its shape is required, U-net can be used to treat this as an image-to-image translation problem.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gicait/centroid-unet">centroid-unet</a> -&gt; Centroid-UNet is deep neural network model to detect centroids from satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/IssamLaradji/cownter_strike">cownter_strike</a> -&gt; counting cows, located with point-annotations, two models: CSRNet (a density-based method) &amp; LCFCN (a detection-based method)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ToyahJade/DO-U-Net">DO-U-Net</a> -&gt; an effective approach for when the size of an object needs to be known, as well as the number of objects in the image, initially created to segment and count Internally Displaced People (IDP) camps in Afghanistan</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/@wongsirikuln/cassava-standing-crop-counting-869cca486ce3" rel="nofollow">Cassava Crop Counting</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gaoguangshuai/Counting-from-Sky-A-Large-scale-Dataset-for-Remote-Sensing-Object-Counting-and-A-Benchmark-Method">Counting from Sky</a> -&gt; A Large-scale Dataset for Remote Sensing Object Counting and A Benchmark Method</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gaoguangshuai/PSGCNet">PSGCNet</a> -&gt; PSGCNet: A Pyramidal Scale and Global Context Guided Network for Dense Object Counting in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gaoguangshuai/psgcnet">psgcnet</a> -&gt; A Pyramidal Scale and Global Context Guided Network for Dense Object Counting in Remote-Sensing Images</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Regression</h2><a id="user-content-regression" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå›å½’" href="#regression"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/regression.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/regression.png" width="300" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Regression prediction of windspeed.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Regression in remote sensing involves predicting continuous variables such as wind speed, tree height, or soil moisture from an image. Both classical machine learning and deep learning approaches can be used to accomplish this task. Classical machine learning utilizes feature engineering to extract numerical values from the input data, which are then used as input for a regression algorithm like linear regression. On the other hand, deep learning typically employs a convolutional neural network (CNN) to process the image data, followed by a fully connected neural network (FCNN) for regression. The FCNN is trained to map the input image to the desired output, providing predictions for the continuous variables of interest. <a href="https://github.com/h-fuzzy-logic/python-windspeed">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/h-fuzzy-logic/python-windspeed">python-windspeed</a> -&gt; Predicting windspeed of hurricanes from satellite images, uses CNN regression in keras</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/23ccozad/hurricane-wind-speed-cnn">hurricane-wind-speed-cnn</a> -&gt; Predicting windspeed of hurricanes from satellite images, uses CNN regression in keras</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/langnico/GEDI-BDL">GEDI-BDL</a> -&gt; Global canopy height regression and uncertainty estimation from GEDI LIDAR waveforms with deep ensembles</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://omdena.com/blog/ai-road-safety/" rel="nofollow">Traffic density estimation as a regression problem instead of object detection</a> -&gt; inspired by paper: Traffic density estimation method from small satellite imagery: Towards frequent remote sensing of car traffic</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/OpticalWaveGauging/OpticalWaveGauging_DNN">OpticalWaveGauging_DNN</a> -&gt; Optical wave gauging using deep neural networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/eio/satellite-pose-estimation">satellite-pose-estimation</a> -&gt; adapts a ResNet50 model architecture to perform pose estimation on several series of satellite images (both real and synthetic)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://mlhub.earth/10.34911/rdnt.xs53up" rel="nofollow">Tropical Cyclone Wind Estimation Competition</a> -&gt; on RadiantEarth MLHub</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mimikuo365/DengueNet-IJCAI">DengueNet</a> -&gt; DengueNet: Dengue Prediction using Spatiotemporal Satellite Imagery for Resource-Limited Countries</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Cloud detection &amp; removal</h2><a id="user-content-cloud-detection--removal" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šäº‘æ£€æµ‹å’Œåˆ é™¤" href="#cloud-detection--removal"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/clouds.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/clouds.png" width="550" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>(left) False colour image and (right) a cloud &amp; shadow mask.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Clouds are a major issue in remote sensing images as they can obscure the underlying ground features. This hinders the accuracy and effectiveness of remote sensing analysis, as the obscured regions cannot be properly interpreted. In order to address this challenge, various techniques have been developed to detect clouds in remote sensing images. Both classical algorithms and deep learning approaches can be employed for cloud detection. Classical algorithms typically use threshold-based techniques and hand-crafted features to identify cloud pixels. However, these techniques can be limited in their accuracy and are sensitive to changes in image appearance and cloud structure. On the other hand, deep learning approaches leverage the power of convolutional neural networks (CNNs) to accurately detect clouds in remote sensing images. These models are trained on large datasets of remote sensing images, allowing them to learn and generalize the unique features and patterns of clouds. The generated cloud mask can be used to identify the cloud pixels and eliminate them from further analysis or, alternatively, cloud inpainting techniques can be used to fill in the gaps left by the clouds. This approach helps to improve the accuracy of remote sensing analysis and provides a clearer view of the ground, even in the presence of clouds. Image adapted from <a href="https://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S1877050922005361" rel="nofollow">this source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/cloudsen12">CloudSEN12</a> -&gt; Sentinel 2 cloud dataset with a <a href="https://github.com/cloudsen12/models">varierty of models here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">From <a href="https://medium.com/sentinel-hub/improving-cloud-detection-with-machine-learning-c09dc5d7cf13" rel="nofollow">this article on sentinelhub</a> there are three popular classical algorithms that detects thresholds in multiple bands in order to identify clouds. In the same article they propose using semantic segmentation combined with a CNN for a cloud classifier (excellent review paper <a href="https://arxiv.org/pdf/1704.06857.pdf" rel="nofollow">here</a>), but state that this requires too much compute resources.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/8/8/666" rel="nofollow">This article</a> compares a number of ML algorithms, random forests, stochastic gradient descent, support vector machines, Bayesian method.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/swlh/segmentation-of-clouds-in-satellite-images-using-deep-learning-a9f56e0aa83d" rel="nofollow">Segmentation of Clouds in Satellite Images Using Deep Learning</a> -&gt; semantic segmentation using a Unet on the Kaggle 38-Cloud dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.azavea.com/blog/2021/02/08/cloud-detection-in-satellite-imagery/" rel="nofollow">Cloud Detection in Satellite Imagery</a> compares FPN+ResNet18 and CheapLab architectures on Sentinel-2 L1C and L2A imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/IPL-UV/DL-L8S2-UV">Benchmarking Deep Learning models for Cloud Detection in Landsat-8 and Sentinel-2 images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/IPL-UV/pvl8dagans">Landsat-8 to Proba-V Transfer Learning and Domain Adaptation for Cloud detection</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/IPL-UV/ee_ipl_uv">Multitemporal Cloud Masking in Google Earth Engine</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/daleroberts/s2cloudmask">s2cloudmask</a> -&gt; Sentinel-2 Cloud and Shadow Detection using Machine Learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sentinel-hub/sentinel2-cloud-detector">sentinel2-cloud-detector</a> -&gt; Sentinel Hub Cloud Detector for Sentinel-2 images in Python</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ameraner/dsen2-cr">dsen2-cr</a> -&gt; cloud removal in Sentinel-2 imagery using a deep residual neural network and SAR-optical data fusion, contains the model code, written in Python/Keras, as well as links to pre-trained checkpoints and the SEN12MS-CR dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/agroimpacts/pyatsa">pyatsa</a> -&gt; Python package implementing the Automated Time-Series Analysis method for masking clouds in satellite imagery developed by Zhu and Helmer 2018</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/CNES/decloud">decloud</a> -&gt; Decloud enables the training of various deep nets to remove clouds in optical image, using e.g. Sentinel 1 &amp; 2</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BradNeuberg/cloudless">cloudless</a> -&gt; Deep learning pipeline for orbital satellite data for detecting clouds</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/remicres/Deep-Gapfill">Deep-Gapfill</a> -&gt; Official implementation of Optical image gap filling using deep convolutional autoencoder from optical and radar images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/cidcom/satellite-cloud-removal-dip">satellite-cloud-removal-dip</a> -&gt; Satellite cloud removal with Deep Image Prior, with <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/14/6/1342" rel="nofollow">paper</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/aliFrancis/cloudFCN">cloudFCN</a> -&gt; Python 3 package for Fully Convolutional Network development, specifically for cloud masking</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/GERSL/Fmask">Fmask</a> -&gt; Fmask (Function of mask) is used for automated clouds, cloud shadows, snow, and water masking for Landsats 4-9 and Sentinel 2 images, in Matlab. Also see <a href="https://github.com/akalenda/PyFmask">PyFmask</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.drivendata.co/blog/cloud-cover-benchmark/" rel="nofollow">HOW TO USE DEEP LEARNING, PYTORCH LIGHTNING, AND THE PLANETARY COMPUTER TO PREDICT CLOUD COVER IN SATELLITE IMAGERY</a></p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/TamirShalev/Clouds-Segmentation-Project">Clouds-Segmentation-Project</a> -&gt; treats as a 3 class problem; Open clouds, Closed clouds and no clouds, uses pytorch on a dataset that consists of IR &amp; Visual Grayscale images</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://benjaminwarner.dev/2022/03/11/detecting-cloud-cover-via-satellite" rel="nofollow">Detecting Cloud Cover Via Sentinel-2 Satellite Data</a> -&gt; blog post on Benjamin Warners Top-10 Percent Solution to DrivenDataâ€™s On CloudN Competition using fast.ai &amp; customized version of XResNeXt50. <a href="https://github.com/warner-benjamin/code_for_blog_posts/tree/main/2022/drivendata_cloudn">Repo</a></p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RSrscoder/AISD">AISD</a> -&gt; Deeply supervised convolutional neural network for shadow detection based on a novel aerial shadow imagery dataset</p>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/andrzejmizera/MEcGANs">MEcGANs</a> -&gt; Cloud Removal from Satellite Imagery using Multispectral Edge-filtered Conditional Generative Adversarial Networks</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/92xianshen/refined-unet-lite">refined-unet-lite</a> -&gt; Refined UNet Lite: End-to-End Lightweight Network for Edge-precise Cloud Detection</p>

</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/cidcom/SatelliteCloudGenerator">SatelliteCloudGenerator</a> -&gt; A PyTorch-based tool to generate clouds for satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/aliFrancis/SEnSeI">SEnSeI</a> -&gt; A python 3 package for developing sensor independent deep learning models for cloud masking in satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/pesekon2/cloud-detection-venus">cloud-detection-venus</a> -&gt; Using Convolutional Neural Networks for Cloud Detection on VENÎ¼S Images over Multiple Land-Cover Types</p>
</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JakobCode/explaining_cloud_effects">explaining_cloud_effects</a> -&gt; Explaining the Effects of Clouds on Remote Sensing Scene Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/DavidHuji/Clouds-Images-Segmentation">Clouds-Images-Segmentation</a> -&gt; Marine Stratocumulus Cloud-Type Classification from SEVIRI Using Convolutional Neural Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/pixiedust18/DeCloud-GAN">DeCloud-GAN</a> -&gt; DeCloud GAN: An Advanced Generative Adversarial Network for Removing Cloud Cover in Optical Remote Sensing Imagery</p>
</li>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Change detection</h2><a id="user-content-change-detection" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šæ›´æ”¹æ£€æµ‹" href="#change-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/change.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/change.png" width="950" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>(left) Initial and (middle) after some development, with (right) the change highlighted.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Change detection is a vital component of remote sensing analysis, enabling the monitoring of landscape changes over time. This technique can be applied to identify a wide range of changes, including land use changes, urban development, coastal erosion, and deforestation. Change detection can be performed on a pair of images taken at different times, or by analyzing multiple images collected over a period of time. It is important to note that while change detection is primarily used to detect changes in the landscape, it can also be influenced by the presence of clouds and shadows. These dynamic elements can alter the appearance of the image, leading to false positives in change detection results. Therefore, it is essential to consider the impact of clouds and shadows on change detection analysis, and to employ appropriate methods to mitigate their influence. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/11/3/240" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wenhwu/awesome-remote-sensing-change-detection">awesome-remote-sensing-change-detection</a> lists many datasets and publications</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MinZHANG-WHU/Change-Detection-Review">Change-Detection-Review</a> -&gt; A review of change detection methods, including code and open data sets for deep learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/change-detection-using-siamese-networks-fc2935fff82" rel="nofollow">Change Detection using Siamese Networks</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/justchenhao/STANet">STANet</a> -&gt;STANet for remote sensing image change detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/annabosman/UNet-based-Unsupervised-Change-Detection">UNet-based-Unsupervised-Change-Detection</a> -&gt; A convolutional neural network (CNN) and semantic segmentation is implemented to detect the changes between the images, as well as classify the changes into the correct semantic class</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/justchenhao/BIT_CD">BIT_CD</a> -&gt; Official Pytorch Implementation of Remote Sensing Image Change Detection with Transformers</p>

</li>

<li>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LiheYoung/SenseEarth2020-ChangeDetection">SenseEarth2020-ChangeDetection</a> -&gt; 1st place solution to the Satellite Image Change Detection Challenge hosted by SenseTime; predictions of five HRNet-based segmentation models are ensembled, serving as pseudo labels of unchanged areas</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/I-Hope-Peace/KPCAMNet">KPCAMNet</a> -&gt; Python implementation of the paper Unsupervised Change Detection in Multi-temporal VHR Images Based on Deep Kernel PCA Convolutional Mapping Network</p>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rulixiang/ChangeDetectionPCAKmeans">ChangeDetectionPCAKmeans</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Change Detection in Satellite Images Using Principal Component Analysis and k-Means Clustering.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/thebinyang/IRCNN">IRCNN</a> -&gt; IRCNN: An Irregular-Time-Distanced Recurrent Convolutional Neural Network for Change Detection in Satellite Time Series</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/thebinyang/UTRNet">UTRNet</a> -&gt; An Unsupervised Time-Distance-Guided Convolutional Recurrent Network for Change Detection in Irregularly Collected Images</p>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/AndreaCodegoni/Tiny_model_4_CD">Tiny_model_4_CD</a> -&gt; TINYCD: A (Not So) Deep Learning Model For Change Detection. Uses LEVIR-CD &amp; WHU-CD datasets</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZSVOS/FHD">FHD</a> -&gt; Feature Hierarchical Differentiation for Remote Sensing Image Change Detection</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.azavea.com/blog/2022/04/18/change-detection-with-raster-vision/" rel="nofollow">Change detection with Raster Vision</a> -&gt; blog post with Colab notebook</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/reglab/building_expansion">building-expansion</a> -&gt; Enhancing Environmental Enforcement with Near Real-Time Monitoring: Likelihood-Based Detection of Structural Expansion of Intensive Livestock Farms</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/justchenhao/SaDL_CD">SaDL_CD</a> -&gt; Semantic-aware Dense Representation Learning for Remote Sensing Image Change Detection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/chen11221/EGCTNet_pytorch">EGCTNet_pytorch</a> -&gt; Building Change Detection Based on an Edge-Guided Convolutional Neural Network Combined with a Transformer</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://git.tu-berlin.de/rsim/S2-cGAN" rel="nofollow">S2-cGAN</a> -&gt; S2-cGAN: Self-Supervised Adversarial Representation Learning for Binary Change Detection in Multispectral Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Chuan-shanjia/A-loss-function-for-change-detection">A-loss-function-for-change-detection</a> -&gt; UAL: Unchanged Area Loss-Function for Change Detection Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yanhengwang-heu/IEEE_TGRS_SSTFormer">IEEE_TGRS_SSTFormer</a> -&gt; Spectralâ€“Spatialâ€“Temporal Transformers for Hyperspectral Image Change Detection</p>
</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wm-Githuber/AFCF3D-Net">AFCF3D-Net</a> -&gt; Adjacent-level Feature Cross-Fusion with 3D CNN for Remote Sensing Image Change Detection</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ChengxiHAN/HANet-CD">HANet-CD</a> -&gt; HANet: A hierarchical attention network for change detection with bi-temporal very-high-resolution remote sensing images</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ChenHongruixuan/SiamCRNN">SiamCRNN</a> -&gt; Change Detection in Multisource VHR Images via Deep Siamese Convolutional Multiple-Layers Recurrent Neural Network</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/utkarshmall13/satellite-change-events">satellite-change-events</a> -&gt; Change Event Dataset for Discovery from Spatio-temporal Remote Sensing Imagery, uses Sentinel 2 CaiRoad &amp; CalFire datasets</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/utkarshmall13/CACo">CACo</a> -&gt; Change-Aware Sampling and Contrastive Learning for Satellite Images</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Dibz15/OpenMineChangeDetection">OpenMineChangeDetection</a> -&gt; Characterising Open Cast Mining from Satellite Data (Sentinel 2), implements TinyCD, LSNet &amp; DDPM-CD</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mpapadomanolaki/multi-task-L-UNet">multi-task-L-UNet</a> -&gt; A Deep Multi-Task Learning Framework Coupling Semantic Segmentation and Fully Convolutional LSTM Networks for Urban Change Detection. Applied to SpaceNet7 dataset</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ChengxiHAN/CGNet-CD">CGNet-CD</a> -&gt; Change Guiding Network: Incorporating Change Prior to Guide Change Detection in Remote Sensing Imagery</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liumency/PA-Former">PA-Former</a> -&gt; PA-Former: Learning Prior-Aware Transformer for Remote Sensing Building Change Detection</p>
</li>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zjd1836/AERNet">AERNet</a> -&gt; AERNet: An Attention-Guided Edge Refinement Network and a Dataset for Remote Sensing Building Change Detection (HRCUS-CD)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Tamer-Saleh/S1GFlood-Detection">S1GFlood-Detection</a> -&gt; DAM-Net: Global Flood Detection from SAR Imagery Using Differential Attention Metric-Based Vision Transformers. Includes S1GFloods dataset</p>
</li>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Time series</h2><a id="user-content-time-series" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šæ—¶é—´åºåˆ—" href="#time-series"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/time-series.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/time-series.png" width="350" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Prediction of the next image in a series.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">The analysis of time series observations in remote sensing data has numerous applications, including enhancing the accuracy of classification models and forecasting future patterns and events. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/13/23/4822" rel="nofollow">Image source</a>. Note: since classifying crops and predicting crop yield are such prominent use case for time series data, these tasks have dedicated sections after this one.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/agr-ayush/Landsat-Time-Series-Analysis-for-Multi-Temporal-Land-Cover-Classification">LANDSAT Time Series Analysis for Multi-temporal Land Cover Classification using Random Forest</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/charlotte-pel/temporalCNN">temporalCNN</a> -&gt; Temporal Convolutional Neural Network for the Classification of Satellite Image Time Series</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VSainteuf/pytorch-psetae">pytorch-psetae</a> -&gt; Satellite Image Time Series Classification with Pixel-Set Encoders and Temporal Self-Attention</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/openclimatefix/satflow">satflow</a> -&gt; optical flow models for predicting future satellite images from current and past ones</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/PiSchool/esa-superresolution-forecasting">esa-superresolution-forecasting</a> -&gt; Forecasting air pollution using ESA Sentinel-5p data, and an encoder-decoder convolutional LSTM neural network architecture</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VSainteuf/lightweight-temporal-attention-pytorch">lightweight-temporal-attention-pytorch</a> -&gt; Light Temporal Attention Encoder (L-TAE) for satellite image time series</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/vwmaus/dtwSat">dtwSat</a> -&gt; Time-Weighted Dynamic Time Warping for satellite image time series analysis</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MarcCoru/MTLCC">MTLCC</a> -&gt; Multitemporal Land Cover Classification Network. A recurrent neural network approach to encode multi-temporal data for land cover classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/PannuMuthu/PWWB">PWWB</a> -&gt; Real-Time Spatiotemporal Air Pollution Prediction with Deep Convolutional LSTM through Satellite Image Analysis</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sarttiso/spaceweather">spaceweather</a> -&gt; predicting geomagnetic storms from satellite measurements of the solar wind and solar corona, uses LSTMs</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/bessammehenni/Forest_wildfire_spreading_convLSTM">Forest_wildfire_spreading_convLSTM</a> -&gt; Modeling of the spreading of forest wildfire using a neural network with ConvLSTM cells. Prediction 3-days forward</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jdiaz4302/ConvTimeLSTM">ConvTimeLSTM</a> -&gt; Extension of ConvLSTM and Time-LSTM for irregularly spaced images, appropriate for Remote Sensing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/NexGenMap/dl-time-series">dl-time-series</a> -&gt; Deep Learning algorithms applied to characterization of Remote Sensing time-series</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jnyborg/tpe">tpe</a> -&gt; Generalized Classification of Satellite Image Time Series With Thermal Positional Encoding</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Orion-AI-Lab/wildfire_forecasting">wildfire_forecasting</a> -&gt; Deep Learning Methods for Daily Wildfire Danger Forecasting. Uses ConvLSTM</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rudolfwilliam/satellite_image_forecasting">satellite_image_forecasting</a> -&gt; predict future satellite images from past ones using features such as precipitation and elevation maps. Entry for the <a href="https://www.earthnet.tech/" rel="nofollow">EarthNet2021</a> challenge</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Agri-Hub/Deep-Learning-for-Cloud-Gap-Filling-on-Normalized-Difference-Vegetation-Index">Deep Learning for Cloud Gap-Filling on Normalized Difference Vegetation Index using Sentinel Time-Series</a> -&gt; A CNN-RNN based model that identifies correlations between optical and SAR data and exports dense Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) time-series of a static 6-day time resolution and can be used for Events Detection tasks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/michaeltrs/DeepSatModels">DeepSatModels</a> -&gt; ViTs for SITS: Vision Transformers for Satellite Image Time Series</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/nasaharvest/presto">Presto</a> -&gt; Lightweight, Pre-trained Transformers for Remote Sensing Timeseries</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/developmentseed/time-series-for-lulc">LULC mapping using time series data &amp; spectral bands</a> -&gt; uses 1D convolutions that learn from time-series data. Accompanies blog post: <a href="https://developmentseed.org/blog/2023-06-29-time-travel-pixels" rel="nofollow">Time-Traveling Pixels: A Journey into Land Use Modeling</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Crop classification</h2><a id="user-content-crop-classification" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šä½œç‰©åˆ†ç±»" href="#crop-classification"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/crops.jpg"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/crops.jpg" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>(left) false colour image and (right) the crop map.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Crop classification in remote sensing is the identification and mapping of different crops in images or sequences of images. It aims to provide insight into the distribution and composition of crops in a specific area, with applications that include monitoring crop growth and evaluating crop damage. Both traditional machine learning methods, such as decision trees and support vector machines, and deep learning techniques, such as convolutional neural networks (CNNs), can be used to perform crop classification. The optimal method depends on the size and complexity of the dataset, the desired accuracy, and the available computational resources. However, the success of crop classification relies heavily on the quality and resolution of the input data, as well as the availability of labeled training data. Image source: High resolution satellite imaging sensors for precision agriculture by Chenghai Yang</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/dida-machine-learning/classification-of-crop-fields-through-satellite-image-time-serie-dida-machine-learning-9b64ce2b8c10" rel="nofollow">Classification of Crop Fields through Satellite Image Time Series</a> -&gt; using a <a href="https://github.com/VSainteuf/pytorch-psetae">pytorch-psetae</a> &amp; Sentinel-2 data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/karimmamer/CropDetectionDL">CropDetectionDL</a> -&gt; using GRU-net, First place solution for Crop Detection from Satellite Imagery competition organized by CV4A workshop at ICLR 2020</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/DariusTheGeek/Radiant-Earth-Spot-the-Crop-Challenge">Radiant-Earth-Spot-the-Crop-Challenge</a> -&gt; The main objective of this challenge was to use time-series of Sentinel-2 multi-spectral data to classify crops in the Western Cape of South Africa. The challenge was to build a machine learning model to predict crop type classes for the test dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/bhavesh907/Crop-Classification">Crop-Classification</a> -&gt; crop classification using multi temporal satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lab-IDEAS/DeepCropMapping">DeepCropMapping</a> -&gt; A multi-temporal deep learning approach with improved spatial generalizability for dynamic corn and soybean mapping, uses LSTM</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lab-IDEAS/CropMappingInterpretation">CropMappingInterpretation</a> -&gt; An interpretation pipeline towards understanding multi-temporal deep learning approaches for crop mapping</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jnyborg/timematch">timematch</a> -&gt; A method to perform unsupervised cross-region adaptation of crop classifiers trained with satellite image time series. We also introduce an open-access dataset for cross-region adaptation with SITS from four different regions in Europe</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MarcCoru/elects">elects</a> -&gt; End-to-End Learned Early Classification of Time Series for In-Season Crop Type Mapping</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://gitlab.com/ignazio.gallo/sentinel-2-time-series-with-3d-fpn-and-time-domain-cai" rel="nofollow">3d-fpn-and-time-domain</a> -&gt; Sentinel 2 Time Series Analysis with 3D Feature Pyramid Network and Time Domain Class Activation Intervals for Crop Mapping</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://gitlab.com/artelabsuper/in-season-and-dynamic-crop-mapping" rel="nofollow">in-season-and-dynamic-crop-mapping</a> -&gt; In-season and dynamic crop mapping using 3D convolution neural networks and sentinel-2 time series, uses the Lombardy crop dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/fmenat/MultiviewCropClassification">MultiviewCropClassification</a> -&gt; A COMPARATIVE ASSESSMENT OF MULTI-VIEW FUSION LEARNING FOR CROP CLASSIFICATION</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Amatofrancesco99/master-thesis">Detection of manure application on crop fields leveraging satellite data and Machine Learning</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tejasri19/Stressnet">StressNet: A spatial-spectral-temporal deformable attention-based framework for water stress classification in maize</a> -&gt; Water Stress Classification on Multispectral data of Maize captured by UAV</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Crop yield</h2><a id="user-content-crop-yield" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå†œä½œç‰©äº§é‡" href="#crop-yield"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/yield.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/yield.png" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Wheat yield data. Blue vertical lines denote observation dates.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Crop yield is a crucial metric in agriculture, as it determines the productivity and profitability of a farm. It is defined as the amount of crops produced per unit area of land and is influenced by a range of factors including soil fertility, weather conditions, the type of crop grown, and pest and disease control. By utilizing time series of satellite images, it is possible to perform accurate crop type classification and take advantage of the seasonal variations specific to certain crops. This information can be used to optimize crop management practices and ultimately improve crop yield. However, to achieve accurate results, it is essential to consider the quality and resolution of the input data, as well as the availability of labeled training data. Appropriate pre-processing and feature extraction techniques must also be employed. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/14/17/4193" rel="nofollow">Image source</a>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JiaxuanYou/crop_yield_prediction">Crop yield Prediction with Deep Learning</a> -&gt; Deep Gaussian Process for Crop Yield Prediction Based on Remote Sensing Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sustainlab-group/Deep-Transfer-Learning-Crop-Yield-Prediction">Deep-Transfer-Learning-Crop-Yield-Prediction</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VaibhavSaini19/Crop-Yield-Prediction-using-ML">Crop-Yield-Prediction-using-ML</a> -&gt; A simple Web application developed in order to provide the farmers/users an approximation on how much amount of crop yield will be produced depending upon the given input</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://omdena.com/blog/yield-prediction/" rel="nofollow">Building a Crop Yield Prediction App in Senegal Using Satellite Imagery and Jupyter Voila</a></p>

<li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Wealth and economic activity</h2><a id="user-content-wealth-and-economic-activity" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè´¢å¯Œå’Œç»æµæ´»åŠ¨" href="#wealth-and-economic-activity"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/economic.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/economic.png" width="450" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>COVID-19 impacts on human and economic activities.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">The traditional approach of collecting economic data through ground surveys is a time-consuming and resource-intensive process. However, advancements in satellite technology and machine learning offer an alternative solution. By utilizing satellite imagery and applying machine learning algorithms, it is possible to obtain accurate and current information on economic activity with greater efficiency. This shift towards satellite imagery-based forecasting not only provides cost savings but also offers a wider and more comprehensive perspective of economic activity. As a result, it is poised to become a valuable asset for both policymakers and businesses. <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2004.07438" rel="nofollow">Image source</a>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.nature.com/articles/s41467-020-16185-w" rel="nofollow">Using publicly available satellite imagery and deep learning to understand economic well-being in Africa, Nature Comms 22 May 2020</a> -&gt; Used CNN on Ladsat imagery (night &amp; day) to predict asset wealth of African villages</p>
</li>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Disaster response</h2><a id="user-content-disaster-response" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç¾éš¾å“åº”" href="#disaster-response"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/disaster.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/disaster.png" width="750" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Detecting buildings destroyed in a disaster.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Remote sensing images are used in disaster response to identify and assess damage to an area. This imagery can be used to detect buildings that are damaged or destroyed, identify roads and road networks that are blocked, determine the size and shape of a disaster area, and identify areas that are at risk of flooding. Remote sensing images can also be used to detect and monitor the spread of forest fires and monitor vegetation health. Also checkout the sections on change detection and water/fire/building segmentation. <a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/blog/ai-helps-detect-disaster-damage-from-satellite-imagery/" rel="nofollow">Image source</a>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">

</li>

Challenge of generalising due to small dataset</p>
