<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Super-resolution</h2><a id="user-content-super-resolution" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè¶…åˆ†è¾¨ç‡" href="#super-resolution"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/super-res.jpg"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/super-res.jpg" width="500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Super resolution using multiple low resolution images as input.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Super-resolution is a technique aimed at improving the resolution of an imaging system. This process can be applied prior to other image processing steps to increase the visibility of small objects or boundaries. Despite its potential benefits, the use of super-resolution is controversial due to the possibility of introducing artifacts that could be mistaken for real features. Super-resolution techniques are broadly categorized into two groups: single image super-resolution (SISR) and multi-image super-resolution (MISR). SISR focuses on enhancing the resolution of a single image, while MISR utilizes multiple images of the same scene to create a high-resolution output. Each approach has its own advantages and limitations, and the choice of method depends on the specific application and desired outcome. <a href="https://github.com/worldstrat/worldstrat">Image source</a>.</p>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Multi image super-resolution (MISR)</h3><a id="user-content-multi-image-super-resolution-misr" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¤šå›¾åƒè¶…åˆ†è¾¨ç‡ï¼ˆMISRï¼‰" href="#multi-image-super-resolution-misr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Note that nearly all the MISR publications resulted from the <a href="https://kelvins.esa.int/proba-v-super-resolution/" rel="nofollow">PROBA-V Super Resolution competition</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/diegovalsesia/deepsum">deepsum</a> -&gt; Deep neural network for Super-resolution of Unregistered Multitemporal images (ESA PROBA-V challenge)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/frandorr/3DWDSRNet">3DWDSRNet</a> -&gt; Satellite Image Multi-Frame Super Resolution (MISR) Using 3D Wide-Activation Neural Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/EscVM/RAMS">RAMS</a> -&gt; Multi-Image Super Resolution of Remotely Sensed Images Using Residual Attention Deep Neural Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Suanmd/TR-MISR">TR-MISR</a> -&gt;  Transformer-based MISR framework for the the PROBA-V super-resolution challenge. With <a href="https://ieeexplore.ieee.org/abstract/document/9684717" rel="nofollow">paper</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ElementAI/HighRes-net">HighRes-net</a> -&gt; Pytorch implementation of HighRes-net, a neural network for multi-frame super-resolution, trained and tested on the European Space Agencyâ€™s Kelvin competition</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/centreborelli/ProbaVref">ProbaVref</a> -&gt; Repurposing the Proba-V challenge for reference-aware super resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/the-missing-ingredient-in-deep-multi-temporal-satellite-image-super-resolution-78cac0f063d9" rel="nofollow">The missing ingredient in deep multi-temporal satellite image super-resolution</a> -&gt; Permutation invariance harnesses the power of ensembles in a single model, with repo <a href="https://github.com/diegovalsesia/piunet">piunet</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/XY-boy/MSTT-STVSR">MSTT-STVSR</a> -&gt; Space-time Super-resolution for Satellite Video: A Joint Framework Based on Multi-Scale Spatial-Temporal Transformer, JAG, 2022</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://centreborelli.github.io/HDR-DSP-SR/" rel="nofollow">Self-Supervised Super-Resolution for Multi-Exposure Push-Frame Satellites</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kuijiang94/DDRN">DDRN</a> -&gt; Deep Distillation Recursive Network for Video Satellite Imagery Super-Resolution</p>
</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto">-<a href="https://github.com/worldstrat/worldstrat">worldstrat</a> -&gt; SISR and MISR implementations of SRCNN</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rarefin/MISR-GRU">MISR-GRU</a> -&gt; Pytorch implementation of MISR-GRU, a deep neural network for multi image super-resolution (MISR), for ProbaV Super Resolution Competition</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/XY-boy/MSDTGP">MSDTGP</a> -&gt; Satellite Video Super-Resolution via Multiscale Deformable Convolution Alignment and Temporal Grouping Projection</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/cedricoeldorf/proba-v-super-resolution-challenge">proba-v-super-resolution-challenge</a> -&gt; Solution to ESA's satellite imagery super resolution challenge</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spicy-mama/PROBA-V-Super-Resolution">PROBA-V-Super-Resolution</a> -&gt; solution using a custom deep learning architecture</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/allenai/satlas-super-resolution">satlas-super-resolution</a> -&gt; Satlas Super Resolution: model is an adaptation of ESRGAN, with changes that allow the input to be a time series of Sentinel-2 images.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/simon-donike/Remote-Sensing-SRGAN">MISR Remote Sensing SRGAN</a> -&gt; PyTorch SRGAN for RGB Remote Sensing imagery, performing both SISR and MISR. MISR implementation inspired by RecursiveNet (HighResNet). Includes pretrained Checkpoints.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Single image super-resolution (SISR)</h3><a id="user-content-single-image-super-resolution-sisr" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå•å›¾åƒè¶…åˆ†è¾¨ç‡ï¼ˆSISRï¼‰" href="#single-image-super-resolution-sisr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Super-resolution - Miscellaneous</h3><a id="user-content-super-resolution---miscellaneous" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè¶…åˆ†è¾¨ç‡ - å…¶ä»–" href="#super-resolution---miscellaneous"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/sentinel-hub/the-value-of-super-resolution-real-world-use-case-2ba811f4cd7f" rel="nofollow">The value of super resolution â€” real world use case</a> -&gt; Medium article on parcel boundary detection with super-resolved satellite imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/super-resolution-on-satellite-imagery-using-deep-learning-part-1-ec5c5cd3cd2" rel="nofollow">Super-Resolution on Satellite Imagery using Deep Learning</a> -&gt; Nov 2016 blog post by CosmiQ Works with a nice introduction to the topic. Proposes and demonstrates a new architecture with perturbation layers with practical guidance on the methodology and <a href="https://github.com/CosmiQ/super-resolution">code</a>. <a href="https://medium.com/the-downlinq/super-resolution-on-satellite-imagery-using-deep-learning-part-3-2e2f61eee1d3" rel="nofollow">Three part series</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/sentinel-hub/the-most-misunderstood-words-in-earth-observation-d0106adbe4b0" rel="nofollow">Introduction to spatial resolution</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ptkin/Awesome-Super-Resolution">Awesome-Super-Resolution</a> -&gt; another 'awesome' repo, getting a little out of date now</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jshermeyer/SR_Utils">Super-Resolution (python) Utilities for managing large satellite images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/isaaccorley/pytorch-enhance">pytorch-enhance</a> -&gt; Library of Image Super-Resolution Models, Datasets, and Metrics for Benchmarking or Pretrained Use. Also <a href="https://github.com/isaaccorley/jax-enhance">checkout this implementation in Jax</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://learnopencv.com/super-resolution-in-opencv/" rel="nofollow">Super Resolution in OpenCV</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/@sistema_gmbh/ai-based-super-resolution-and-change-detection-to-enforce-sentinel-2-systematic-usage-65aa37d0365" rel="nofollow">AI-based Super resolution and change detection to enforce Sentinel-2 systematic usage</a> -&gt; Worldview-2 images (2m) were used to create a reference dataset and increase the spatial resolution of the Copernicus sensor from 10m to 5m</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liumency/SRCDNet">SRCDNet</a> -&gt; Super-resolution-based Change Detection Network with Stacked Attention Module for Images with Different Resolutions. SRCDNet is designed to learn and predict change maps from bi-temporal images with different resolutions</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/chengerr/Model-Guided-Deep-Hyperspectral-Image-Super-resolution">Model-Guided Deep Hyperspectral Image Super-resolution</a> -&gt; code accompanying the paper: Model-Guided Deep Hyperspectral Image Super-Resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/smpetrie/superres">Super-resolving beyond satellite hardware</a> -&gt; <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2103.06270" rel="nofollow">paper</a> assessing SR performance in reconstructing realistically degraded satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/KellyYutongHe/satellite-pixel-synthesis-pytorch">satellite-pixel-synthesis-pytorch</a> -&gt; PyTorch implementation of NeurIPS 2021 paper: Spatial-Temporal Super-Resolution of Satellite Imagery via Conditional Pixel Synthesis</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/bostankhan6/SRE-HAN">SRE-HAN</a> -&gt; Squeeze-and-Residual-Excitation Holistic Attention Network improves super-resolution (SR) on remote-sensing imagery compared to other state-of-the-art attention-based SR models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/deephdc/satsr">satsr</a> -&gt; A project to perform super-resolution on multispectral images from any satellite, including Sentinel 2, Landsat 8, VIIRS &amp;MODIS</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wjwjww/OLI2MSI">OLI2MSI</a> -&gt; dataset for remote sensing imagery super-resolution composed of Landsat8-OLI and Sentinel2-MSI images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/palmdong/MMSR">MMSR</a> -&gt; Learning Mutual Modulation for Self-Supervised Cross-Modal Super-Resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liangjiandeng/HSRnet">HSRnet</a> -&gt; Hyperspectral Image Super-resolution via Deep Spatio-spectral Attention Convolutional Neural Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dongrunmin/RRSGAN">RRSGAN</a> -&gt; RRSGAN: Reference-Based Super-Resolution for Remote Sensing Image</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/centreborelli/HDR-DSP-SR">HDR-DSP-SR</a> -&gt; Self-supervised multi-image super-resolution for push-frame satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZhuangChen25674/GAN-HSI-SR">GAN-HSI-SR</a> -&gt; Hyperspectral Image Super-Resolution by Band Attention Through Adversarial Learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/restoring-old-aerial-images-with-deep-learning-60f0cfd2658" rel="nofollow">Restoring old aerial images with Deep Learning</a> -&gt; Medium article Super Resolution with Perceptual Loss function and real images as input</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Pansharpening</h2><a id="user-content-pansharpening" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå…¨è‰²é”åŒ–" href="#pansharpening"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/pansharpen.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/pansharpen.png" width="500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Pansharpening example with a resolution difference of factor 4.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Pansharpening is a data fusion method that merges the high spatial detail from a high-resolution panchromatic image with the rich spectral information from a lower-resolution multispectral image. The result is a single, high-resolution color image that retains both the sharpness of the panchromatic band and the color information of the multispectral bands. This process enhances the spatial resolution while preserving the spectral qualities of the original images. <a href="https://www.researchgate.net/publication/308121983_Computer_Vision_for_Large_Format_Digital_Aerial_Cameras" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto">Several algorithms described <a href="http://desktop.arcgis.com/en/arcmap/10.3/manage-data/raster-and-images/fundamentals-of-panchromatic-sharpening.htm" rel="nofollow">in the ArcGIS docs</a>, with the simplest being taking the mean of the pan and RGB pixel value.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Zeyu-Zhu/PGCU">PGCU</a> -&gt; Probability-based Global Cross-modal Upsampling for Pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mapbox/rio-pansharpen">rio-pansharpen</a> -&gt; pansharpening Landsat scenes</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ThomasWangWeiHong/Simple-Pansharpening-Algorithms">Simple-Pansharpening-Algorithms</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yuanmaoxun/Working-For-Pansharpening">Working-For-Pansharpening</a> -&gt; long list of pansharpening methods and update of <a href="https://github.com/Lihui-Chen/Awesome-Pansharpening">Awesome-Pansharpening</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liuqingjie/PSGAN">PSGAN</a> -&gt; A Generative Adversarial Network for Remote Sensing Image Pan-sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ThomasWangWeiHong/Pansharpening-by-Convolutional-Neural-Network">Pansharpening-by-Convolutional-Neural-Network</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/dbuscombe-usgs/PBR_filter">PBR_filter</a> -&gt; Pansharpening by Background Removal algorithm for sharpening RGB images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/codegaj/py_pansharpening">py_pansharpening</a> -&gt; multiple algorithms implemented in python</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xyc19970716/Deep-Learning-PanSharpening">Deep-Learning-PanSharpening</a> -&gt; deep-learning based pan-sharpening code package, we reimplemented include PNN, MSDCNN, PanNet, TFNet, SRPPNN, and our purposed network DIPNet</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wgcban/HyperTransformer">HyperTransformer</a> -&gt; A Textural and Spectral Feature Fusion Transformer for Pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wgcban/DIP-HyperKite">DIP-HyperKite</a> -&gt; Hyperspectral Pansharpening Based on Improved Deep Image Prior and Residual Reconstruction</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Meiqi-Gong/D2TNet">D2TNet</a> -&gt; A ConvLSTM Network with Dual-direction Transfer for Pan-sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/esertel/PanColorGAN-VHR-Satellite-Images">PanColorGAN-VHR-Satellite-Images</a> -&gt; Rethinking CNN-Based Pansharpening: Guided Colorization of Panchromatic Images via GANs</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/andrewekhalel/MTL_PAN_SEG">MTL_PAN_SEG</a> -&gt; Multi-task deep learning for satellite image pansharpening and segmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/matciotola/Z-PNN">Z-PNN</a> -&gt; Pansharpening by convolutional neural networks in the full resolution framework</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HaoZhang1018/GTP-PNet">GTP-PNet</a> -&gt; GTP-PNet: A residual learning network based on gradient transformation prior for pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/XiaoXiao-Woo/UDL">UDL</a> -&gt; Dynamic Cross Feature Fusion for Remote Sensing Pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yisun98/PSData">PSData</a> -&gt; A Large-Scale General Pan-sharpening DataSet, which contains PSData3 (QB, GF-2, WV-3) and PSData4 (QB, GF-1, GF-2, WV-2).</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yisun98/AFPN">AFPN</a> -&gt; Adaptive Detail Injection-Based Feature Pyramid Network For Pan-sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yisun98/pan-sharpening">pan-sharpening</a> -&gt; multiple methods demonstrated for multispectral and panchromatic images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhysora/PSGan-Family">PSGan-Family</a> -&gt; PSGAN: A Generative Adversarial Network for Remote Sensing Image Pan-Sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/oyam/PanNet-Landsat">PanNet-Landsat</a> -&gt; A Deep Network Architecture for Pan-Sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liangjiandeng/DLPan-Toolbox">DLPan-Toolbox</a> -&gt;  Machine Learning in Pansharpening: A Benchmark, from Shallow to Deep Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ChengJin-git/LPPN">LPPN</a> -&gt; Laplacian pyramid networks: A new approach for multispectral pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hvn2/S2_SSC_CNN">S2_SSC_CNN</a> -&gt; Zero-shot Sentinel-2 Sharpening Using A Symmetric Skipped Connection Convolutional Neural Network</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hvn2/S2S_UCNN">S2S_UCNN</a> -&gt; Sentinel 2 sharpening using a single unsupervised convolutional neural network with MTF-Based degradation model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RSMagneto/SSE-Net">SSE-Net</a> -&gt; Spatial and Spectral Extraction Network With Adaptive Feature Fusion for Pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhysora/UCGAN">UCGAN</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Cycle-consistent Generative Adversarial Networks for Pan-sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Keyu-Yan/GCPNet">GCPNet</a> -&gt; When Pansharpening Meets Graph Convolution Network and Knowledge Distillation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhysora/PanFormer">PanFormer</a> -&gt; PanFormer: a Transformer Based Model for Pan-sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/nithin-gr/Pansharpening">Pansharpening</a> -&gt; Pansformers: Transformer-Based Self-Attention Network for Pansharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/purijs/Sentinel-2-Superresolution">Sentinel-2 Band Pan-Sharpening</a></p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Image-to-image translation</h2><a id="user-content-image-to-image-translation" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå›¾åƒåˆ°å›¾åƒçš„ç¿»è¯‘" href="#image-to-image-translation"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/translation.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/translation.png" width="500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>(left) Sentinel-1 SAR input, (middle) translated to RGB and (right) Sentinel-2 true RGB image for comparison.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Image-to-image translation is a crucial aspect of computer vision that utilizes machine learning models to transform an input image into a new, distinct output image. In the field of remote sensing, it plays a significant role in bridging the gap between different imaging domains, such as converting Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) images into RGB (Red Green Blue) images. This technology has a wide range of applications, including improving image quality, filling in missing information, and facilitating cross-domain image analysis and comparison. By leveraging deep learning algorithms, image-to-image translation has become a powerful tool in the arsenal of remote sensing researchers and practitioners. <a href="https://www.researchgate.net/publication/335648375_SAR-to-Optical_Image_Translation_Using_Supervised_Cycle-Consistent_Adversarial_Networks" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/how-to-develop-a-pix2pix-gan-for-image-to-image-translation/" rel="nofollow">How to Develop a Pix2Pix GAN for Image-to-Image Translation</a> -&gt; how to develop a Pix2Pix model for translating satellite photographs to Google map images. A good intro to GANS</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.washington.edu/news/2021/04/21/a-growing-problem-of-deepfake-geography-how-ai-falsifies-satellite-images/" rel="nofollow">A growing problem of â€˜deepfake geographyâ€™: How AI falsifies satellite images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.kaggle.com/alincijov/pix2pix-maps" rel="nofollow">Kaggle Pix2Pix Maps</a> -&gt; dataset for pix2pix to take a google map satellite photo and build a street map</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tuezato/guided-deep-decoder">guided-deep-decoder</a> -&gt; With guided deep decoder, you can solve different image pair fusion problems, allowing super-resolution, pansharpening or denoising</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/paulaharder/hackathon-ci-2020">hackathon-ci-2020</a> -&gt; generate nighttime imagery from infrared observations</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/anonymous-ai-for-earth/satellite-to-satellite-translation">satellite-to-satellite-translation</a> -&gt; VAE-GAN architecture for unsupervised image-to-image translation with shared spectral reconstruction loss. Model is trained on GOES-16/17 and Himawari-8 L1B data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/greed2411/unet_pytorch">Pytorch implementation of UNet for converting aerial satellite images into google maps kinda images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Misaliet/Seamless-Satellite-image-Synthesis">Seamless-Satellite-image-Synthesis</a> -&gt; generate abitrarily large RGB images from a map</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://machinelearningmastery.com/how-to-develop-a-pix2pix-gan-for-image-to-image-translation/" rel="nofollow">How to Develop a Pix2Pix GAN for Image-to-Image Translation</a> -&gt; article on machinelearningmastery.com</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/anh-nn01/Satellite-Imagery-to-Map-Translation-using-Pix2Pix-GAN-framework">Satellite-Imagery-to-Map-Translation-using-Pix2Pix-GAN-framework</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/summitgao/RSIT_SRM_ISD">RSIT_SRM_ISD</a> -&gt; PyTorch implementation of Remote sensing image translation via style-based recalibration module and improved style discriminator</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/manishemirani/pix2pix_google_maps">pix2pix_google_maps</a> -&gt; Converts satellite images to map images using pix2pix models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/enomotokenji/sar2color-igarss2018-chainer">sar2color-igarss2018-chainer</a> -&gt; Image Translation Between Sar and Optical Imagery with Generative Adversarial Nets</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JakobSig/HSI2RGB">HSI2RGB</a> -&gt; Create realistic looking RGB images using remote sensing hyperspectral images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/shagunuppal/sat_to_map">sat_to_map</a> -&gt; Learning mappings to generate city maps images from corresponding satellite images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/shashi7679/pix2pix-GANs">pix2pix-GANs</a> -&gt; Generate Map using Satellite Image &amp; PyTorch</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/miquel-espinosa/map-sat">map-sat</a> -&gt; Generate Your Own Scotland: Satellite Image Generation Conditioned on Maps</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Data fusion</h2><a id="user-content-data-fusion" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šæ•°æ®èåˆ" href="#data-fusion"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/fusion.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/fusion.png" width="800" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Illustration of a fusion workflow.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Data fusion is a technique for combining information from different sources such as Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR), optical imagery, and non-imagery data such as Internet of Things (IoT) sensor data. The integration of diverse data sources enables data fusion to overcome the limitations of individual sources, leading to the creation of models that are more accurate and informative than those constructed from a single source. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/14/18/4458" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/px39n/Awesome-Data-Fusion-for-Remote-Sensing">Awesome-Data-Fusion-for-Remote-Sensing</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JiaxinLiCAS/UDALN_GRSL">UDALN_GRSL</a> -&gt; Deep Unsupervised Blind Hyperspectral and Multispectral Data Fusion</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ellaampy/CropTypeMapping">CropTypeMapping</a> -&gt; Crop type mapping from optical and radar (Sentinel-1&amp;2) time series using attention-based deep learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/likyoo/Multimodal-Remote-Sensing-Toolkit">Multimodal-Remote-Sensing-Toolkit</a> -&gt; uses Hyperspectral and LiDAR Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/m-hamza-mughal/Aerial-Template-Matching">Aerial-Template-Matching</a> -&gt; development of an algorithm for template Matching on aerial imagery applied to UAV dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SebastianHafner/DS_UNet">DS_UNet</a> -&gt; Sentinel-1 and Sentinel-2 Data Fusion for Urban Change Detection using a Dual Stream U-Net, uses Onera Satellite Change Detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SebastianHafner/DDA_UrbanExtraction">DDA_UrbanExtraction</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Domain Adaptation for Global Urban Extraction using Sentinel-1 and Sentinel-2 Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LouisChen0104/swinstfm">swinstfm</a> -&gt; Remote Sensing Spatiotemporal Fusion using Swin Transformer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Junjue-Wang/LoveCS">LoveCS</a> -&gt; Cross-sensor domain adaptation for high-spatial resolution urban land-cover mapping: from airborne to spaceborne imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/aysim/comingdowntoearth">comingdowntoearth</a> -&gt; Implementation of 'Coming Down to Earth: Satellite-to-Street View Synthesis for Geo-Localization'</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/giovgiac/neptune">Matching between acoustic and satellite images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zorzi-s/MapRepair">MapRepair</a> -&gt; Deep Cadastre Maps Alignment and Temporal Inconsistencies Fix in Satellite Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rahulgite94/Compressive-Sensing-and-Deep-Learning-Framework">Compressive-Sensing-and-Deep-Learning-Framework</a> -&gt;  Compressive Sensing is used as an initial guess to combine data from multiple sources, with LSTM used to refine the result</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wangxiaodiu/DeepSim">DeepSim</a> -&gt; DeepSIM: GPS Spoofing Detection on UAVs using Satellite Imagery Matching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/XieQi2015/MHF-net">MHF-net</a> -&gt; Multispectral and Hyperspectral Image Fusion by MS/HS Fusion Net</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/huangshanshan33/Remote_Sensing_Image_Fusion">Remote_Sensing_Image_Fusion</a> -&gt; Semi-Supervised Remote Sensing Image Fusion Using Multi-Scale Conditional Generative Adversarial network with Siamese Structure</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yyyyangyi/CNNs-for-Multi-Source-Remote-Sensing-Data-Fusion">CNNs for Multi-Source Remote Sensing Data Fusion</a> -&gt; Single-stream CNN with Learnable Architecture for Multi-source Remote Sensing Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Cervest/ds-generative-reflectance-fusion">Deep Generative Reflectance Fusion</a> -&gt; Achieving Landsat-like reflectance at any date by fusing Landsat and MODIS surface reflectance with deep generative models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/danfenghong/IEEE_TGRS_MDL-RS">IEEE_TGRS_MDL-RS</a> -&gt;  More Diverse Means Better: Multimodal Deep Learning Meets Remote-Sensing Imagery Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hw2hwei/SSRNET">SSRNET</a> -&gt; SSR-NET: Spatial-Spectral Reconstruction Network for Hyperspectral and Multispectral Image Fusion</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kregmi/cross-view-image-matching">cross-view-image-matching</a> -&gt; Bridging the Domain Gap for Ground-to-Aerial Image Matching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WeiTan1992/CoF-MSMG-PCNN">CoF-MSMG-PCNN</a> -&gt; Remote Sensing Image Fusion via Boundary Measured Dual-Channel PCNN in Multi-Scale Morphological Gradient Domain</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mrk1992/robust_matching_network_on_remote_sensing_imagery_pytorch">robust_matching_network_on_remote_sensing_imagery_pytorch</a> -&gt; A Robust Matching Network for Gradually Estimating Geometric Transformation on Remote Sensing Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/theonegis/edcstfn">edcstfn</a> -&gt; An Enhanced Deep Convolutional Model for Spatiotemporal Image Fusion</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/theonegis/ganstfm">ganstfm</a> -&gt; A Flexible Reference-Insensitive Spatiotemporal Fusion Model for Remote Sensing Images Using Conditional Generative Adversarial Network</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/DocF/CMAFF">CMAFF</a> -&gt; Cross-Modality Attentive Feature Fusion for Object Detection in Multispectral Remote Sensing Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yisun98/SOLC">SOLC</a> -&gt; MCANet: A joint semantic segmentation framework of optical and SAR images for land use classification. Uses <a href="https://github.com/AmberHen/WHU-OPT-SAR-dataset">WHU-OPT-SAR-dataset</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/AnkurDeria/MFT">MFT</a> -&gt; Multimodal Fusion Transformer for Remote Sensing Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/danfenghong/ISPRS_S2FL">ISPRS_S2FL</a> -&gt; Multimodal Remote Sensing Benchmark Datasets for Land Cover Classification with A Shared and Specific Feature Learning Model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yuvalofek/HSHT-Satellite-Imagery-Synthesis">HSHT-Satellite-Imagery-Synthesis</a> -&gt; Improving Flood Maps by Increasing the Temporal Resolution of Satellites Using Hybrid Sensor Fusion</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Kasra2020/MDC">MDC</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Data Fusion With Deeper Perspective: A Novel Multisensor Deep Clustering Algorithm</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ShivamP1993/FusAtNet">FusAtNet</a> -&gt; FusAtNet: Dual Attention based SpectroSpatial Multimodal Fusion Network for Hyperspectral and LiDAR Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/oktaykarakus/ReSIF/tree/main/AMM-FuseNet">AMM-FuseNet</a> -&gt; Attention-Based Multi-Modal Image Fusion Network for Land Cover Mapping</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/caohuimin/MANet">MANet</a> -&gt; MANet: A Network Architecture for Remote Sensing Spatiotemporal Fusion Based on Multiscale and Attention Mechanisms</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Julia90/DCSA-Net">DCSA-Net</a> -&gt; Dynamic Convolution Self-Attention Network for Land-Cover Classification in VHR Remote-Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/felferrari/deforestation-from-data-fusion">deforestation-from-data-fusion</a> -&gt; Fusing Sentinel-1 and Sentinel-2 images for deforestation detection in the Brazilian Amazon under diverse cloud conditions</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://git.tu-berlin.de/rsim/sct-fusion" rel="nofollow">sct-fusion</a> -&gt; Transformer-based Multi-Modal Learning for Multi Label Remote Sensing Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/EarthNets/RSI-MMSegmentation">RSI-MMSegmentation</a> -&gt; GAMUS: A Geometry-aware Multi-modal Semantic Segmentation Benchmark for Remote Sensing Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/isaaccorley/dfc2022-baseline">dfc2022-baseline</a> -&gt; baseline solution to the 2022 IEEE GRSS Data Fusion Contest (DFC2022) using TorchGeo, PyTorch Lightning, and Segmentation Models PyTorch to train a U-Net with a ResNet-18 backbone and a loss function of Focal + Dice loss to perform semantic segmentation on the DFC2022 dataset</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Generative networks</h2><a id="user-content-generative-networks" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šç”Ÿæˆç½‘ç»œ" href="#generative-networks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/gan.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/gan.png" width="500" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Example generated images using a GAN.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Generative networks (e.g. GANs) aim to generate new, synthetic data that appears similar to real-world data. This generated data can be used for a wide range of purposes, including data augmentation, data imbalance correction, and filling in missing or corrupted data. Including generating synthetic data can improve the performance of remote sensing algorithms and models, leading to more accurate and reliable results. <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2207.14580" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/radiant-earth-insights/using-generative-adversarial-networks-to-address-scarcity-of-geospatial-training-data-e61cacec986e" rel="nofollow">Using Generative Adversarial Networks to Address Scarcity of Geospatial Training Data</a> -&gt; GAN perform better than CNN in segmenting land cover classes outside of the training dataset (article, no code)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lixiang-ucas/Building-A-Nets">Building-A-Nets</a> -&gt; robust building extraction from high-resolution remote sensing images with adversarial networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ualsg/GANmapper">GANmapper</a> -&gt; a building footprint generator using Generative Adversarial Networks</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wangle53/CSA-CDGAN">CSA-CDGAN</a> -&gt; Channel Self-Attention Based Generative Adversarial Network for Change Detection of Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lzhengchun/DSGAN">DSGAN</a> -&gt; a conditinal GAN for dynamic precipitation downscaling</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kheyer/MarsGAN">MarsGAN</a> -&gt; GAN trained on satellite photos of Mars</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/summitgao/HC_ADGAN">HC_ADGAN</a> -&gt; codes for the paper Adaptive Dropblock Enhanced GenerativeAdversarial Networks for Hyperspectral Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LendelTheGreat/SCALAE">SCALAE</a> -&gt; Formatting the Landscape: Spatial conditional GAN for varying population in satellite imagery. Method to generate satellite imagery from custom 2D population maps</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tailongnguyen/Satellite-Image-Forgery-Detection-and-Localization">Satellite-Image-Forgery-Detection-and-Localization</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ermongroup/STGAN">STGAN</a> -&gt; PyTorch Implementation of STGAN for Cloud Removal in Satellite Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Cervest/ds-gan-spatiotemporal-evaluation">ds-gan-spatiotemporal-evaluation</a> -&gt; evaluating use of deep generative models in remote sensing applications</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/awweide/pub-ffi-gan">pub-ffi-gan</a> -&gt; Applying generative adversarial networks for anomaly detection in hyperspectral remote sensing imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/weihancug/GAN-based-HRRS-Sample-Generation-for-Image-Classification">GAN-based method to generate high-resolution remote sensing for data augmentation and image classification</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/aashishrai3799/Remote-Sensing-Image-Generation">Remote-Sensing-Image-Generation</a> -&gt; Generate RS Images using Generative Adversarial Networks (GAN)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LANMNG/RoadDA">RoadDA</a> -&gt; Stagewise Unsupervised Domain Adaptation with Adversarial Self-Training for Road Segmentation of Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhysora/PSGan-Family">PSGan-Family</a> -&gt; A Generative Adversarial Network for Remote Sensing Image Pan-Sharpening</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Oarowolo11/11785-Project">Satellite Image Augmetation with GANs</a> -&gt; Image Augmentation for Satellite Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zzh811/opt2sar-cyclegan">opt2sar-cyclegan</a> -&gt; Research on SAR image generation method based on non-homologous data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/softwaremill/sentinel-cgan">sentinel-cgan</a> -&gt; code for <a href="https://blog.softwaremill.com/generative-adversarial-networks-in-satellite-image-datasets-augmentation-b7045d2f51ab" rel="nofollow">article</a>: Generative adversarial networks in satellite image datasets augmentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mlundine/Shoreline_Extraction_GAN">Shoreline_Extraction_GAN</a> -&gt; Shoreline extraction via generative adversarial networks, prediction via LSTMs</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Rohit18/Landsat8-Sentinel2-Fusion">Landsat8-Sentinel2-Fusion</a> -&gt; Translating Landsat 8 to Sentinel-2 using a GAN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RubenGres/Seg2Sat">Seg2Sat</a> -&gt; Seg2Sat explores the potential of diffusion algorithms such as StableDiffusion and ControlNet to generate aerial images based on terrain segmentation data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MuhammedM294/SAR2Optical">SAR2Optical</a> -&gt; Transcoding Sentinel-1 SAR to Sentinel-2 using cGAN</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Autoencoders, dimensionality reduction, image embeddings &amp; similarity search</h2><a id="user-content-autoencoders-dimensionality-reduction-image-embeddings--similarity-search" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè‡ªåŠ¨ç¼–ç å™¨ã€é™ç»´ã€å›¾åƒåµŒå…¥å’Œç›¸ä¼¼æ€§æœç´¢" href="#autoencoders-dimensionality-reduction-image-embeddings--similarity-search"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/autoencoder.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/autoencoder.png" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Example of using an autoencoder to create a low dimensional representation of hyperspectral data.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Autoencoders are a type of neural network that aim to simplify the representation of input data by compressing it into a lower dimensional form. This is achieved through a two-step process of encoding and decoding, where the encoding step compresses the data into a lower dimensional representation, and the decoding step restores the data back to its original form. The goal of this process is to reduce the data's dimensionality, making it easier to store and process, while retaining the essential information. Dimensionality reduction, as the name suggests, refers to the process of reducing the number of dimensions in a dataset. This can be achieved through various techniques such as principal component analysis (PCA) or singular value decomposition (SVD). Autoencoders are one type of neural network that can be used for dimensionality reduction. In the field of computer vision, image embeddings are vector representations of images that capture the most important features of the image. These embeddings can then be used to perform similarity searches, where images are compared based on their features to find similar images. This process can be used in a variety of applications, such as image retrieval, where images are searched based on certain criteria like color, texture, or shape. It can also be used to identify duplicate images in a dataset. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/11/7/864" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/autoencoders-their-application-in-remote-sensing-95f6e2bc88f" rel="nofollow">Autoencoders &amp; their Application in Remote Sensing</a> -&gt; intro article and example use case applied to SAR data for land classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/meghshukla/LEt-SNE">LEt-SNE</a> -&gt; Dimensionality Reduction and visualization technique that compensates for the curse of dimensionality</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/autoencoders-for-land-cover-classification-of-hyperspectral-images-part-1-c3c847ebc69b" rel="nofollow">AutoEncoders for Land Cover Classification of Hyperspectral Images</a> -&gt; An autoencoder nerual net is used to reduce 103 band data to 60 features (dimensionality reduction), keras. Also read <a href="https://syamkakarla.medium.com/auto-encoders-for-land-cover-classification-in-hyperspectral-images-part-2-f8978d443d6d" rel="nofollow">part 2</a> which implements K-NNC, SVM and Gradient Boosting</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spaceml-org/Image-Similarity-Search">Image-Similarity-Search</a> -&gt; an app that helps perform super fast image retrieval on PyTorch models for better embedding space interpretability</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spaceml-org/Interactive-TSNE">Interactive-TSNE</a> -&gt; a tool that provides a way to visually view a PyTorch model's feature representation for better embedding space interpretability</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://blog.tensorflow.org/2020/04/how-airbus-detects-anomalies-iss-telemetry-data-tfx.html" rel="nofollow">How Airbus Detects Anomalies in ISS Telemetry Data Using TFX</a> -&gt; uses an autoencoder</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ultysim/RoofNet">RoofNet</a> -&gt; identify roof age using historical satellite images to lower the customer acquisition cost for new solar installations. Uses a VAE: Variational Autoencoder</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2002.02624" rel="nofollow">Visual search over billions of aerial and satellite images</a> -&gt; implemented <a href="https://blog.descarteslabs.com/geovisual-search-for-rapid-generation-of-annotated-datasets" rel="nofollow">at Descartes labs</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/uber-research/parallax">parallax</a> -&gt; Tool for interactive embeddings visualization</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/remicres/Deep-Gapfill">Deep-Gapfill</a> -&gt; Official implementation of Optical image gap filling using deep convolutional autoencoder from optical and radar images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/fisch92/Metric-embeddings-for-satellite-image-classification">Mxnet repository for generating embeddings on satellite images</a> -&gt; Includes sampling of images, mining algorithms, different architectures, error functions, measures for evaluation.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://huggingface.co/blog/fine-tune-clip-rsicd" rel="nofollow">Fine tuning CLIP with Remote Sensing (Satellite) images and captions</a> -&gt; fine tuning CLIP on the <a href="https://github.com/201528014227051/RSICD_optimal">RSICD</a> image captioning dataset, to enable querying large catalogues in natural language. With <a href="https://github.com/arampacha/CLIP-rsicd">repo</a>, uses ğŸ¤—</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://huggingface.co/blog/image-search-datasets" rel="nofollow">Image search with ğŸ¤— datasets</a> -&gt; tutorial on fine tuning an image search model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/FlorenceJiang/SynImageAnalysis">SynImageAnalysis</a> -&gt; comparing synthetic and real satellite images in the latent feature space (embeddings)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jiankang1991/GRN-SNDL">GRN-SNDL</a> -&gt; model the relations between samples (or scenes) by making use of a graph structure which is fed into network learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jiankang1991/SauMoCo">SauMoCo</a> -&gt; Deep Unsupervised Embedding for Remotely Sensed Images Based on Spatially Augmented Momentum Contrast</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jiankang1991/TGRS_RiDe">TGRS_RiDe</a> -&gt; Rotation Invariant Deep Embedding for RemoteSensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spaceml-org/RaVAEn">RaVAEn</a> -&gt; RaVAEn is a lightweight, unsupervised approach for change detection in satellite data based on Variational Auto-Encoders (VAEs) with the specific purpose of on-board deployment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/martenjostmann/deep-discrete-image-retrieval">Reverse image search using deep discrete feature extraction and locality-sensitive hashing</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jiankang1991/SNCA_CE">SNCA_CE</a> -&gt; Deep Metric Learning based on Scalable Neighborhood Components for Remote Sensing Scene Characterization</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/shulavkarki/LandslideDetection-from-satellite-imagery">LandslideDetection-from-satellite-imagery</a> -&gt; Using Attention and Autoencoder boosted CNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/vladan-stojnic/split-brain-remote-sensing">split-brain-remote-sensing</a> -&gt; Analysis of Color Space Quantization in Split-Brain Autoencoder for Remote Sensing Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/up42/image-similarity-measures">image-similarity-measures</a> -&gt; Implementation of eight evaluation metrics to access the similarity between two images. <a href="https://up42.com/blog/tech/image-similarity-measures" rel="nofollow">Blog post here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sdhayalk/Large_Scale_GeoVisual_Search">Large_Scale_GeoVisual_Search</a> -&gt; ResNet architecture on UC Merced Land Use Dataset with hamming distance for similarity based search</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JakeForsey/geobacter">geobacter</a> -&gt; Generates useful feature embeddings for geospatial locations</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/kunnalparihar/Satellite-Image-Segmentation">Satellite-Image-Segmentation</a> -&gt; the KV-Net model uses this feature of autoencoders to reconnect the disconnected roads</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VNDhanush/Satellite-Image-Enhancement">Satellite-Image-Enhancement</a> -&gt; Image enhancement using GAN's and autoencoders</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RayanAAY-ops/Variational-Autoencoder-For-Satellite-Imagery">Variational-Autoencoder-For-Satellite-Imagery</a> -&gt; a special VAE to squeeze N images into one single representation with colors segmentating the different objects</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gher-ulg/DINCAE">DINCAE</a> -&gt; Data-Interpolating Convolutional Auto-Encoder is a neural network to reconstruct missing data in satellite observations</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ekalinicheva/3D_SITS_Clustering">3D_SITS_Clustering</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Satellite Image Time Series Clustering Using Object-Based Approaches and 3D Convolutional Autoencoder</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/GDSL-UL/sat_cnn">sat_cnn</a> -&gt; Estimating Generalized Measures of Local Neighbourhood Context from Multispectral Satellite Images Using a Convolutional Neural Network. Uses a convolutional autoencoder (CAE)</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZhouMengjie/you-are-here">you-are-here</a> -&gt; You Are Here: Geolocation by Embedding Maps and Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tensorflow/similarity">Tensorflow similarity</a> -&gt; offers state-of-the-art algorithms for metric learning and all the necessary components to research, train, evaluate, and serve similarity-based models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://docs.lightly.ai/tutorials/package/tutorial_simsiam_esa.html" rel="nofollow">Train SimSiam on Satellite Images</a> using lightly.ai to generate embeddings that can be used for data exploration and understanding</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WillieMaddox/Airbus_SDC_dup">Airbus_SDC_dup</a> -&gt; Project focused on detecting duplicate regions of overlapping satellite imagery. Applied to Airbus ship detection dataset</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/bair-climate-initiative/scale-mae">scale-mae</a> -&gt; Scale-MAE: A Scale-Aware Masked Autoencoder for Multiscale Geospatial Representation Learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/microsoft/satclip">satclip</a> -&gt; A Global, General-Purpose Geographic Location Encoder from Microsoft</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Image retrieval</h2><a id="user-content-image-retrieval" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå›¾åƒæ£€ç´¢" href="#image-retrieval"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/retrieval.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/retrieval.png" width="550" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Illustration of the remote sensing image retrieval process.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Image retrieval is the task of retrieving images from a collection that are similar to a query image. Image retrieval plays a vital role in remote sensing by enabling the efficient and effective search for relevant images from large image archives, and by providing a way to quantify changes in the environment over time. <a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/12/2/219" rel="nofollow">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/weiweisong415/Demo_AHCL_for_TGRS2022">Demo_AHCL_for_TGRS2022</a> -&gt; Asymmetric Hash Code Learning (AHCL) for remote sensing image retrieval</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xiaoyuan1996/GaLR">GaLR</a> -&gt; Remote Sensing Cross-Modal Text-Image Retrieval Based on Global and Local Information</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xiaoyuan1996/retrievalSystem">retrievalSystem</a> -&gt; cross-modal image retrieval system</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xiaoyuan1996/AMFMN">AMFMN</a> -&gt; Exploring a Fine-grained Multiscale Method for Cross-modal Remote Sensing Image Retrieval</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/flateon/Active-Learning-for-Remote-Sensing-Image-Retrieval">Active-Learning-for-Remote-Sensing-Image-Retrieval</a> -&gt; unofficial implementation of paper: A Novel Active Learning Method in Relevance Feedback for Content-Based Remote Sensing Image Retrieval</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ushasi/CMIR-NET-A-deep-learning-based-model-for-cross-modal-retrieval-in-remote-sensing">CMIR-NET</a> -&gt; A deep learning based model for cross-modal retrieval in remote sensing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/smallsmallflypigtang/Deep-Hash-learning-for-Remote-Sensing-Image-Retrieval">Deep-Hash-learning-for-Remote-Sensing-Image-Retrieval</a> -&gt; Deep Hash Learning for Remote Sensing Image Retrieval</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MLEnthusiast/MHCLN">MHCLN</a> -&gt; Deep Metric and Hash-Code Learning for Content-Based Retrieval of Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lannguyen0910/HydroViet_VOR">HydroViet_VOR</a> -&gt; Object Retrieval in satellite images with Triplet Network</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/AICyberTeam/AMFMN">AMFMN</a> -&gt; Exploring a Fine-Grained Multiscale Method for Cross-Modal Remote Sensing Image Retrieval</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Image Captioning</h2><a id="user-content-image-captioning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå›¾åƒæ ‡é¢˜" href="#image-captioning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p align="center" dir="auto">
  <a target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" href="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/blob/master/images/captioned.png"><img src="/satellite-image-deep-learning/techniques/raw/master/images/captioned.png" width="600" style="max-width: 100%;"></a>
  <br>
  <b>Example captioned image.</b>
</p>
<p dir="auto">Image Captioning is the task of automatically generating a textual description of an image. In remote sensing, image captioning can be used to automatically generate captions for satellite or aerial images, which can be useful for a variety of purposes, such as image search and retrieval, data cataloging, and data dissemination. The generated captions can provide valuable information about the content of the images, including the location, the type of terrain or objects present, and the weather conditions, among others. This information can be used to quickly and easily understand the content of the images, without having to manually examine each image. <a href="https://github.com/chan64/remote_sensing_image_captioning">Image source</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/iOPENCap/awesome-remote-image-captioning">awesome-remote-image-captioning</a> -&gt; a list of awesome remote sensing image captioning resources</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/geoaigroup/awesome-vision-language-models-for-earth-observation">awesome-vision-language-models-for-earth-observation</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Junjue-Wang/CapFormer">CapFormer</a> -&gt; Pure transformer for remote sensing image caption</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/chan64/remote_sensing_image_captioning">remote_sensing_image_captioning</a> -&gt; Region Driven Remote Sensing Image Captioning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hiteshK03/Remote-sensing-image-captioning-with-transformer-and-multilabel-classification">Remote Sensing Image Captioning with Transformer and Multilabel Classification</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ushasi/Siamese-spatial-Graph-Convolution-Network">Siamese-spatial-Graph-Convolution-Network</a> -&gt; Siamese graph convolutional network for content based remote sensing image retrieval</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Chen-Yang-Liu/MLAT">MLAT</a> -&gt; Remote-Sensing Image Captioning Based on Multilayer Aggregated Transformer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hw2hwei/WordSent">WordSent</a> -&gt; Wordâ€“Sentence Framework for Remote Sensing Image Captioning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Meditation0119/a-mask-guided-transformer-with-topic-token-for-remote-sensing-image-captioning">a-mask-guided-transformer-with-topic-token</a> -&gt; A Mask-Guided Transformer Network with Topic Token for Remote Sensing Image Captioning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/QiaoqiaoYang/MetaCaptioning">Meta captioning</a> -&gt; A meta learning based remote sensing image captioning framework</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/TalentBoy2333/remote-sensing-image-caption">remote-sensing-image-caption</a> -&gt; image classification and image caption by PyTorch</p>

<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://huggingface.co/blog/fine-tune-clip-rsicd" rel="nofollow">Fine tuning CLIP with Remote Sensing (Satellite) images and captions</a> -&gt; fine tuning CLIP on the <a href="https://github.com/201528014227051/RSICD_optimal">RSICD</a> image captioning dataset, to enable querying large catalogues in natural language. With <a href="https://github.com/arampacha/CLIP-rsicd">repo</a>, uses ğŸ¤—. Also read <a href="https://dienhoa.github.io/dhblog/posts/finetune_clip.html" rel="nofollow">Why and How to Fine-tune CLIP</a></p>
</li>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Visual Question Answering</h2><a id="user-content-visual-question-answering" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè§†è§‰é—®ç­”" href="#visual-question-answering"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Visual Question Answering (VQA) is the task of automatically answering a natural language question about an image. In remote sensing, VQA enables users to interact with the images and retrieve information using natural language questions. For example, a user could ask a VQA system questions such as "What is the type of land cover in this area?", "What is the dominant crop in this region?" or "What is the size of the city in this image?". The system would then analyze the image and generate an answer based on its understanding of the image content.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://gitlab.lrz.de/ai4eo/reasoning/VQA-easy2hard" rel="nofollow">VQA-easy2hard</a> -&gt; From Easy to Hard: Learning Language-guided Curriculum for Visual Question Answering on Remote Sensing Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://git.tu-berlin.de/rsim/lit4rsvqa" rel="nofollow">lit4rsvqa</a> -&gt; LiT-4-RSVQA: Lightweight Transformer-based Visual Question Answering in Remote Sensing</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Mixed data learning</h2><a id="user-content-mixed-data-learning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šæ··åˆæ•°æ®å­¦ä¹ " href="#mixed-data-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Mixed data learning is the process of learning from datasets that may contain an mix of images, textual and numeric data. Mixed data learning can help improve the accuracy of models by allowing them to learn from multiple sources at once and use more sophisticated methods to identify patterns and correlations.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/teaching-a-neural-network-to-see-roads-74bff240c3e5" rel="nofollow">Predicting the locations of traffic accidents with satellite imagery and convolutional neural networks</a> -&gt; Combining satellite imagery and structured data to predict the location of traffic accidents with a neural network of neural networks, with <a href="https://github.com/L-Lewis/Predicting-traffic-accidents-CNN">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://rosenfelder.ai/multi-input-neural-network-pytorch/" rel="nofollow">Multi-Input Deep Neural Networks with PyTorch-Lightning - Combine Image and Tabular Data</a> -&gt; excellent intro article using pytorch, not actually applied to satellite data but to real estate data, with <a href="https://github.com/MarkusRosen/pytorch_multi_input_example">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/1705.06057" rel="nofollow">Joint Learning from Earth Observation and OpenStreetMap Data to Get Faster Better Semantic Maps</a> -&gt; fusion based architectures and coarse-to-fine segmentation to include the OpenStreetMap layer into multispectral-based deep fully convolutional networks, arxiv paper</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.tensorflow.org/decision_forests/tutorials/model_composition_colab" rel="nofollow">Composing Decision Forest and Neural Network models</a> tensorflow documentation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.pyimagesearch.com/2019/02/04/keras-multiple-inputs-and-mixed-data/" rel="nofollow">pyimagesearch article on mixed-data</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jrzaurin/pytorch-widedeep">pytorch-widedeep</a> -&gt; A flexible package for multimodal-deep-learning to combine tabular data with text and images using Wide and Deep models in Pytorch</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/songtaohe/accidentRiskMap">accidentRiskMap</a> -&gt; Inferring high-resolution traffic accident risk maps based on satellite imagery and GPS trajectories</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://research.facebook.com/blog/2023/4/every-tree-counts-large-scale-mapping-of-canopy-height-at-the-resolution-of-individual-trees/" rel="nofollow">Sub-meter resolution canopy height map by Meta</a> -&gt; Satellite Metadata combined with outputs from simple CNN to regress canopy height</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Few &amp; zero shot learning</h2><a id="user-content-few--zero-shot-learning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¾ˆå°‘å’Œé›¶æœºä¼šå­¦ä¹ " href="#few--zero-shot-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">This is a class of techniques which attempt to make predictions for classes with few, one or even zero examples provided during training. In zero shot learning (ZSL) the model is assisted by the provision of auxiliary information which typically consists of descriptions/semantic attributes/word embeddings for both the seen and unseen classes at train time (<a href="https://learnopencv.com/zero-shot-learning-an-introduction/" rel="nofollow">ref</a>). These approaches are particularly relevant to remote sensing, where there may be many examples of common classes, but few or even zero examples for other classes of interest.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/geoaigroup/Aerial-SAM">Aerial-SAM</a> -&gt; Zero-Shot Refinement of Buildingsâ€™ Segmentation Models using SAM</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lixiang-ucas/FSODM">FSODM</a> -&gt; Few-shot Object Detection on Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.mdpi.com/2072-4292/13/1/108/htm" rel="nofollow">Few-Shot Classification of Aerial Scene Images via Meta-Learning</a> -&gt; 2020 publication, a classification model that can quickly adapt to unseen categories using only a few labeled samples</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lx709/Few-shot-Learning-Meta-Learning-on-Remote-Sensing-Papers">Papers about Few-shot Learning / Meta-Learning on Remote Sensing</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zoraup/SPNet">SPNet</a> -&gt; Siamese-Prototype Network for Few-Shot Remote Sensing Image Scene Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/sjliu68/MDL4OW">MDL4OW</a> -&gt; Few-Shot Hyperspectral Image Classification With Unknown Classes Using Multitask Deep Learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Ybowei/P-CNN">P-CNN</a> -&gt; Prototype-CNN for Few-Shot Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Li-ZK/CIR-FSD-2022">CIR-FSD-2022</a> -&gt; Context Information Refinement for Few-Shot Object Detection in Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/YuxiangZhang-BIT/IEEE_TNNLS_Gia-CFSL">IEEE_TNNLS_Gia-CFSL</a> -&gt; Graph Information Aggregation Cross-Domain Few-Shot Learning for Hyperspectral Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/B-Xi/TIP_2022_CMFSL">TIP_2022_CMFSL</a> -&gt; Few-shot Learning with Class-Covariance Metric for Hyperspectral Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MarcCoru/sen12ms-human-few-shot-classifier">sen12ms-human-few-shot-classifier</a> -&gt; Humans are poor few-shot classifiers for Sentinel-2 land cover</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZhaohuiXue/S3Net">S3Net</a> -&gt; S3Net: Spectralâ€“Spatial Siamese Network for Few-Shot Hyperspectral Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jjwwczy/jjwwczy-SiameseNet-for-few-shot-Hyperspectral-Classification">SiameseNet-for-few-shot-Hyperspectral-Classification</a> -&gt; 3DCSN:SiameseNet-for-few-shot-Hyperspectral-Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/OMEGAFSL/MESSL">MESSL</a> -&gt; Multiform Ensemble Self-Supervised Learning for Few-Shot Remote Sensing Scene Classification</p>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Self-supervised, unsupervised &amp; contrastive learning</h2><a id="user-content-self-supervised-unsupervised--contrastive-learning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè‡ªæˆ‘ç›‘ç£ã€æ— ç›‘ç£å’Œå¯¹æ¯”å­¦ä¹ " href="#self-supervised-unsupervised--contrastive-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Self-supervised, unsupervised &amp; contrastive learning are all methods of machine learning that use unlabeled data to train algorithms. Self-supervised learning uses labeled data to create an artificial supervisor, while unsupervised learning uses only the data itself to identify patterns and similarities. Contrastive learning uses pairs of data points to learn representations of data, usually for classification tasks. Note that self-supervised approaches are commonly used in the training of so-called Foundational models, since they enable learning from large quantities of unlablleded data, tyipcally time series.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://devblog.pytorchlightning.ai/seasonal-contrast-transferable-visual-representations-for-remote-sensing-73a17863ed07" rel="nofollow">Seasonal Contrast: Unsupervised Pre-Training from Uncurated Remote Sensing Data</a> -&gt; Seasonal Contrast (SeCo) is an effective pipeline to leverage unlabeled data for in-domain pre-training of remote sensing representations. Models trained with SeCo achieve better performance than their ImageNet pre-trained counterparts and state-of-the-art self-supervised learning methods on multiple downstream tasks. <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2103.16607" rel="nofollow">paper</a> and <a href="https://github.com/ElementAI/seasonal-contrast">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://omdena.com/blog/land-cover-classification/" rel="nofollow">Unsupervised Learning for Land Cover Classification in Satellite Imagery</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://ermongroup.github.io/blog/tile2vec/" rel="nofollow">Tile2Vec: Unsupervised representation learning for spatially distributed data</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/descarteslabs/contrastive_sensor_fusion">Contrastive Sensor Fusion</a> -&gt; Code implementing Contrastive Sensor Fusion, an approach for unsupervised learning of multi-sensor representations targeted at remote sensing imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lloydwindrim/hyperspectral-autoencoders">hyperspectral-autoencoders</a> -&gt; Tools for training and using unsupervised autoencoders and supervised deep learning classifiers for hyperspectral data, built on tensorflow. Autoencoders are unsupervised neural networks that are useful for a range of applications such as unsupervised feature learning and dimensionality reduction.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/sentinel-2-image-clustering-in-python-58f7f2c8a7f6" rel="nofollow">Sentinel-2 image clustering in python</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/BUPTLdy/MARTA-GAN">MARTA GANs: Unsupervised Representation Learning for Remote Sensing Image Classification</a></p>
</li>
<li>
