<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Weakly &amp; semi-supervised learning</h2><a id="user-content-weakly--semi-supervised-learning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¼±ç›‘ç£å­¦ä¹ å’ŒåŠç›‘ç£å­¦ä¹ " href="#weakly--semi-supervised-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Weakly &amp; semi-supervised learning are two methods of machine learning that use both labeled and unlabeled data for training. Weakly supervised learning uses weakly labeled data, which may be incomplete or inaccurate, while semi-supervised learning uses both labeled and unlabeled data. Weakly supervised learning is typically used in situations where labeled data is scarce and unlabeled data is abundant. Semi-supervised learning is typically used in situations where labeled data is abundant but also contains some noise or errors. Both techniques can be used to improve the accuracy of machine learning models by making use of additional data sources.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VMarsocci/MARE">MARE</a> -&gt; self-supervised Multi-Attention REsu-net for semantic segmentation in remote sensing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/weihancug/SSGF-for-HRRS-scene-classification">SSGF-for-HRRS-scene-classification</a> -&gt; A semi-supervised generative framework with deep learning features for high-resolution remote sensing image scene classification</p>
</li>

</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/alhichri/SSDAN">SSDAN</a> -&gt; Multi-Source Semi-Supervised Domain Adaptation Network for Remote Sensing Scene Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jiankang1991/HR-S2DML">HR-S2DML</a> -&gt; High-Rankness Regularized Semi-Supervised Deep Metric Learning for Remote Sensing Imagery</p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/B-Xi/TNNLS_2022_X-GPN">TNNLS_2022_X-GPN</a> -&gt; Semisupervised Cross-scale Graph Prototypical Network for Hyperspectral Image Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/LobellLab/weakly_supervised">weakly_supervised</a> -&gt; Weakly Supervised Deep Learning for Segmentation of Remote Sensing Imagery. Demonstrates that segmentation can be performed using small datasets comprised of pixel or image labels</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/engrjavediqbal/wan">wan</a> -&gt; Weakly-Supervised Domain Adaptation for Built-up Region Segmentation in Aerial and Satellite Imagery</p>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Active learning</h2><a id="user-content-active-learning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šä¸»åŠ¨å­¦ä¹ " href="#active-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Supervised deep learning techniques typically require a huge number of annotated/labelled examples to provide a training dataset. However labelling at scale take significant time, expertise and resources. Active learning techniques aim to reduce the total amount of annotation that needs to be performed by selecting the most useful images to label from a large pool of unlabelled images, thus reducing the time to generate useful training datasets. These processes may be referred to as <a href="https://medium.com/pytorch/https-medium-com-robert-munro-active-learning-with-pytorch-2f3ee8ebec" rel="nofollow">Human-in-the-Loop Machine Learning</a></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2101.02480" rel="nofollow">Active learning for object detection in high-resolution satellite images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/microsoft/aerial_wildlife_detection">AIDE V2 - Tools for detecting wildlife in aerial images using active learning</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/grant-m-s/AstronomicAL">AstronomicAL</a> -&gt; An interactive dashboard for visualisation, integration and classification of data using Active Learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Follow tutorials for <a href="https://docs.lightly.ai/docs/active-learning-yolov7" rel="nofollow">active learning for object detection</a> <a href="https://docs.lightly.ai/docs/active-learning-for-driveable-area-segmentation-using-cityscapes" rel="nofollow">and segmentation</a> on the lightly platform.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/spaceml-org/Active-Labeler">Active-Labeler by spaceml-org</a> -&gt; a CLI Tool that facilitates labeling datasets with just a SINGLE line of code</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/agroimpacts/labeller">Labelling platform for Mapping Africa active learning project</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/previtus/ChangeDetectionProject">ChangeDetectionProject</a> -&gt; Trying out Active Learning in with deep CNNs for Change detection on remote sensing data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/immuno121/ALS4GAN">ALS4GAN</a> -&gt; Active Learning for Improved Semi Supervised Semantic Segmentation in Satellite Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/flateon/Active-Learning-for-Remote-Sensing-Image-Retrieval">Active-Learning-for-Remote-Sensing-Image-Retrieval</a> -&gt; unofficial implementation of paper: A Novel Active Learning Method in Relevance Feedback for Content-Based Remote Sensing Image Retrieval</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/alteia-ai/DIAL">DIAL</a> -&gt; DIAL: Deep Interactive and Active Learning for Semantic Segmentation in Remote Sensing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/microsoft/whales">whales</a> -&gt; An active learning pipeline for identifying whales in high-resolution satellite imagery, by Microsoft</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Federated learning</h2><a id="user-content-federated-learning" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šè”é‚¦å­¦ä¹ " href="#federated-learning"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Federated learning is an approach to distributed machine learning where a central processor coordinates the training of an individual model in each of its clients. It is a type of distributed ML which means that the data is distributed among different devices or locations and the model is trained on all of them. The central processor aggregates the model updates from all the clients and then sends the global model parameters back to the clients. This is done to protect the privacy of data, as the data remains on the local device and only the global model parameters are shared with the central processor. This technique can be used to train models with large datasets that cannot be stored in a single device, as well as to enable certain privacy-preserving applications.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/anandcu3/Federated-Learning-for-Remote-Sensing">Federated-Learning-for-Remote-Sensing</a> -&gt;  implementation of three Federated Learning models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/PratikGarai/Semantic-Segmentation-UNet-Federated">Semantic-Segmentation-UNet-Federated</a> -&gt; FedUKD: Federated UNet Model with Knowledge Distillation for Land Use Classification from Satellite and Street Views</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://git.tu-berlin.de/rsim/MM-FL" rel="nofollow">MM-FL</a> -&gt; Learning Across Decentralized Multi-Modal Remote Sensing Archives with Federated Learning</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Transformers</h2><a id="user-content-transformers" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå˜å½¢é‡‘åˆš" href="#transformers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Vision transformers are state-of-the-art models for vision tasks such as image classification and object detection. They differ from CNNs as they use self-attention instead of convolution to learn global relations between all pixels in the image. Vision transformers employ a transformer encoder architecture, composed of multi-layer blocks with multi-head self-attention and feed-forward layers, enabling the capture of rich contextual information for more accurate predictions.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VIROBO-15/Transformer-in-Remote-Sensing">Transformer-in-Remote-Sensing</a> -&gt; Transformers in Remote Sensing: A Survey</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ViTAE-Transformer/Remote-Sensing-RVSA">Remote-Sensing-RVSA</a> -&gt; Advancing Plain Vision Transformer Towards Remote Sensing Foundation Model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/antofuller/SatViT">SatViT</a> -&gt; self-supervised training of multispectral optical and SAR vision transformers</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Levantespot/UDA_for_RS">UDA_for_RS</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Domain Adaptation for Remote Sensing Semantic Segmentation with Transformer</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://myrtle.ai/learn/leo-1-low-earth-orbit-satellites/" rel="nofollow">Vision Transformers for Low Earth Orbit Satellites</a> -&gt; blog post that investigates deploying Vision Transformers on low earth orbit satellites</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Adversarial ML</h2><a id="user-content-adversarial-ml" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå¯¹æŠ—æ€§æœºå™¨å­¦ä¹ " href="#adversarial-ml"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Efforts to detect falsified images &amp; deepfakes</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/YonghaoXu/UAE-RS">UAE-RS</a> -&gt; dataset that provides black-box adversarial samples in the remote sensing field</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xuxiangsun/PSGAN">PSGAN</a> -&gt; Perturbation Seeking Generative Adversarial Networks: A Defense Framework for Remote Sensing Image Scene Classification</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/YonghaoXu/SACNet">SACNet</a> -&gt; Self-Attention Context Network: Addressing the Threat of Adversarial Attacks for Hyperspectral Image Classification</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Image registration</h2><a id="user-content-image-registration" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šå›¾åƒæ³¨å†Œ" href="#image-registration"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Image registration is the process of registering one or more images onto another (typically well georeferenced) image. Traditionally this is performed manually by identifying control points (tie-points) in the images, for example using QGIS. This section lists approaches which mostly aim to automate this manual process. There is some overlap with the data fusion section but the distinction I make is that image registration is performed as a prerequisite to downstream processes which will use the registered data as an input.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Image_registration" rel="nofollow">Wikipedia article on registration</a> -&gt; register for change detection or <a href="https://mono.software/2018/03/14/Image-stitching/" rel="nofollow">image stitching</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phase_correlation" rel="nofollow">Phase correlation</a> is used to estimate the XY translation between two images with sub-pixel accuracy. Can be used for accurate registration of low resolution imagery onto high resolution imagery, or to register a <a href="https://www.mathworks.com/help/images/registering-an-image-using-normalized-cross-correlation.html" rel="nofollow">sub-image on a full image</a> -&gt; Unlike many spatial-domain algorithms, the phase correlation method is resilient to noise, occlusions, and other defects. With <a href="https://scikit-image.org/docs/dev/auto_examples/registration/plot_register_rotation.html" rel="nofollow">additional pre-processing</a> image rotation and scale changes can also be calculated.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/sentinel-hub/how-to-co-register-temporal-stacks-of-satellite-images-5167713b3e0b" rel="nofollow">How to Co-Register Temporal Stacks of Satellite Images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jandremarais/ImageRegistration">ImageRegistration</a> -&gt; Interview assignment for multimodal image registration using SIFT</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/matejak/imreg_dft">imreg_dft</a> -&gt; Image registration using discrete Fourier transform. Given two images it can calculate the difference between scale, rotation and position of imaged features. Used by the <a href="https://up42.com/marketplace/blocks/processing/up42-coregistration" rel="nofollow">up42 co-registration service</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://danschef.git-pages.gfz-potsdam.de/arosics/doc/about.html" rel="nofollow">arosics</a> -&gt; Perform automatic subpixel co-registration of two satellite image datasets using phase-correlation, XY translations only.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/vldkhramtsov/SubpixelAlignment">SubpixelAlignment</a> -&gt; Implementation of tiff image alignment through phase correlation for pixel- and subpixel-bias</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yzhq97/cnn-registration">cnn-registration</a> -&gt; A image registration method using convolutional neural network features written in Python2, Tensorflow 1.5</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/simon-donike/Siamese_ShiftNet">Siamese_ShiftNet</a> -&gt; NN predicting spatial coregistration shift of remote sensing imagery. Adapted from HighRes-net</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ily-R/ImageCoregistration">ImageCoregistration</a> -&gt; Image registration with openCV using sift and RANSAC</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Lydorn/mapalignment">mapalignment</a> -&gt; Aligning and Updating Cadaster Maps with Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/placeforyiming/CVPR21-Deep-Lucas-Kanade-Homography">CVPR21-Deep-Lucas-Kanade-Homography</a> -&gt; deep learning pipeline to accurately align challenging multimodality images. The method is based on traditional Lucas-Kanade algorithm with feature maps extracted by deep neural networks.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://eo-learn.readthedocs.io/en/latest/_modules/eolearn/coregistration/coregistration.html" rel="nofollow">eolearn</a> implements phase correlation, feature matching and <a href="https://learnopencv.com/image-alignment-ecc-in-opencv-c-python/" rel="nofollow">ECC</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://matthewearl.github.io/2021/03/06/mars2020-reproject/" rel="nofollow">Reprojecting the Perseverance landing footage onto satellite imagery</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Kornia provides <a href="https://kornia.readthedocs.io/en/latest/applications/image_registration.html" rel="nofollow">image registration</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zju3dv/LoFTR">LoFTR</a> -&gt; Detector-Free Local Feature Matching with Transformers. Good performance matching satellite image pairs, tryout the web demo on your data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://gitlab.orfeo-toolbox.org/remote_modules/image-to-db-registration" rel="nofollow">image-to-db-registration</a> -&gt; This remote module implements an algorithm for automated vector Database registration onto an Image. Implemented in the orfeo-toolbox</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MrPingQi/MS_HLMO_registration">MS_HLMO_registration</a> -&gt; Multi-scale Histogram of Local Main Orientation for Remote Sensing Image Registration, with <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2204.00260" rel="nofollow">paper</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lan-cz/cnn-matching">cnn-matching</a> -&gt; Deep learning algorithm for feature matching of cross modality remote sensing images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/geoyee/Imatch-P">Imatch-P</a> -&gt; A demo using SuperGlue and SuperPoint to do the image matching task based PaddlePaddle</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/xuyingxiao/NBR-Net">NBR-Net</a> -&gt; A Non-rigid Bi-directional Registration Network for Multi-temporal Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/woshiybc/Multi-Scale-Unsupervised-Framework-MSUF">MU-Net</a> -&gt; A Multi-Scale Framework with Unsupervised Learning for Remote Sensing Image Registration</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/tynguyen/unsupervisedDeepHomographyRAL2018">unsupervisedDeepHomographyRAL2018</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Deep Homography applied to aerial data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhangliukun/registration_cnn_ntg">registration_cnn_ntg</a> -&gt; A Multispectral Image Registration Method Based on Unsupervised Learning</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liliangzhi110/remote-sensing-images-registration-dataset">remote-sensing-images-registration-dataset</a> -&gt; at 0.23m, 3.75m &amp; 30m resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/liliangzhi110/semantictemplatematching">semantic-template-matching</a> -&gt; A deep learning semantic template matching framework for remote sensing image registration</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ei1994/GMN-Generative-Matching-Network">GMN-Generative-Matching-Network</a> -&gt; Deep Generative Matching Network for Optical and SAR Image Registration</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/system123/SOMatch">SOMatch</a> -&gt; A deep learning framework for matching of SAR and optical imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/dronehub/datasets-96fc4f9a92e5" rel="nofollow">Interspectral image registration dataset</a> -&gt; including satellite and drone imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lan-cz/RISG-image-matching">RISG-image-matching</a> -&gt; A rotation invariant SuperGlue image matching algorithm</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jaehyunnn/DeepAerialMatching_pytorch">DeepAerialMatching_pytorch</a> -&gt; A Two-Stream Symmetric Network with Bidirectional Ensemble for Aerial Image Matching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ZJU-Robotics-Lab/DPCN">DPCN</a> -&gt; Deep Phase Correlation for End-to-End Heterogeneous Sensor Measurements Matching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Dmmm1997/FSRA">FSRA</a> -&gt; A Transformer-Based Feature Segmentation and Region Alignment Method For UAV-View Geo-Localization</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/imdumpl78/IHN">IHN</a> -&gt; Iterative Deep Homography Estimation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhanghan9718/OSMNet">OSMNet</a> -&gt; Explore Better Network Framework for High-Resolution Optical and SAR Image Matching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/TheKiteFlier/L2_Siamese">L2_Siamese</a> -&gt; Registration of Multiresolution Remote Sensing Images Based on L2-Siamese Model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mpapadomanolaki/Multi-Step-Deformable-Registration">Multi-Step-Deformable-Registration</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Multi-Step Deformable Registration of Remote Sensing Imagery based on Deep Learning</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Terrain mapping, Disparity Estimation, Lidar, DEMs &amp; NeRF</h2><a id="user-content-terrain-mapping-disparity-estimation-lidar-dems--nerf" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šåœ°å½¢æµ‹ç»˜ã€è§†å·®ä¼°è®¡ã€æ¿€å…‰é›·è¾¾ã€DEM å’Œ NeRF" href="#terrain-mapping-disparity-estimation-lidar-dems--nerf"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Measure surface contours &amp; locate 3D points in space from 2D images. NeRF stands for Neural Radiance Fields and is the term used in deep learning communities to describe a model that generates views of complex 3D scenes based on a partial set of 2D images</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Digital_elevation_model" rel="nofollow">Wikipedia DEM article</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Phase_correlation" rel="nofollow">phase correlation</a> article</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/IntelRealSense/librealsense/blob/master/doc/depth-from-stereo.md">Intro to depth from stereo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Map terrain from stereo images to produce a digital elevation model (DEM) -&gt; high resolution &amp; paired images required, typically 0.3 m, e.g. <a href="https://dg-cms-uploads-production.s3.amazonaws.com/uploads/document/file/37/DG-WV2ELEVACCRCY-WP.pdf" rel="nofollow">Worldview</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Process of creating a DEM <a href="https://www.int-arch-photogramm-remote-sens-spatial-inf-sci.net/XLI-B1/327/2016/isprs-archives-XLI-B1-327-2016.pdf" rel="nofollow">here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="http://pro.arcgis.com/en/pro-app/help/data/imagery/generate-elevation-data-using-the-dems-wizard.htm" rel="nofollow">ArcGIS can generate DEMs from stereo images</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/centreborelli/s2p">S2P</a> -&gt; S2P is a Python library and command line tool that implements a stereo pipeline which produces elevation models from images taken by high resolution optical satellites such as PlÃ©iades, WorldView, QuickBird, Spot or Ikonos.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/geohackweek/glacierhack_2018">Predict the fate of glaciers</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mrharicot/monodepth">monodepth - Unsupervised single image depth prediction with CNNs</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jzbontar/mc-cnn">Stereo Matching by Training a Convolutional Neural Network to Compare Image Patches</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/giswqs/lidar">Terrain and hydrological analysis based on LiDAR-derived digital elevation models (DEM) - Python package</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://scikit-image.org/docs/0.13.x/auto_examples/transform/plot_register_translation.html" rel="nofollow">Phase correlation in scikit-image</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VMarsocci/3DCD">3DCD</a> -&gt; Inferring 3D change detection from bitemporal optical images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://docs.mapbox.com/help/troubleshooting/access-elevation-data/" rel="nofollow">The Mapbox API</a> provides images and elevation maps, <a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/creating-high-resolution-satellite-images-with-mapbox-and-python-750b3ac83dd7" rel="nofollow">article here</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/geoai/reconstructing-3d-buildings-from-aerial-lidar-with-ai-details-6a81cb3079c0" rel="nofollow">Reconstructing 3D buildings from aerial LiDAR with Mask R-CNN</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/stuckerc/ResDepth">ResDepth</a> -&gt; A Deep Prior For 3D Reconstruction From High-resolution Satellite Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.drivendata.org/competitions/78/overhead-geopose-challenge/" rel="nofollow">overhead-geopose-challenge</a> -&gt; competition to build computer vision algorithms that can effectively model the height and pose of ground objects for monocular satellite images taken from oblique angles. Blog post <a href="https://www.drivendata.co/blog/overhead-geopose-challenge-winners/" rel="nofollow">MEET THE WINNERS OF THE OVERHEAD GEOPOSE CHALLENGE</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/CNES/cars">cars</a> -&gt; a dedicated and open source 3D tool to produce Digital Surface Models from satellite imaging by photogrammetry. This Multiview stereo pipeline is intended for massive DSM production with a robust and performant design</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Panagiotou/ImageToDEM">ImageToDEM</a> -&gt; Generating Elevation Surface from a Single RGB Remotely Sensed Image Using a U-Net for generator and a PatchGAN for the discriminator</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/speed8928/IMELE">IMELE</a> -&gt; Building Height Estimation from Single-View Aerial Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mikeskaug/ridges">ridges</a> -&gt; deep semantic segmentation model for identifying ridges in topography</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/disbr007/planet_tools">planet_tools</a> -&gt; Selection of imagery from Planet API for creation of stereo elevation models</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Kai-46/SatelliteNeRF">SatelliteNeRF</a> -&gt; PyTorch-based Neural Radiance Fields adapted to satellite domain</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Kai-46/SatelliteSfM">SatelliteSfM</a> -&gt; A library for solving the satellite structure from motion problem</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/SBCV/SatelliteSurfaceReconstruction">SatelliteSurfaceReconstruction</a> -&gt; 3D Surface Reconstruction From Multi-Date Satellite Images, ISPRS, 2021</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/giovgiac/son2sat">son2sat</a> -&gt; A neural network coded in TensorFlow 1 that produces satellite images from acoustic images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/marcelampc/aerial_mtl">aerial_mtl</a> -&gt; PyTorch implementation for multi-task learning with aerial images to learn both semantics and height from aerial image datasets; fuses RGB &amp; lidar</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/MacOS/ReKlaSat-3D">ReKlaSat-3D</a> -&gt; 3D Reconstruction and Classification from Very High Resolution Satellite Imagery</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/lauraset/BuildingHeightModel">M3Net</a> -&gt; A deep learning method for building height estimation using high-resolution multi-view imagery over urban areas</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Sheng029/HMSM-Net">HMSM-Net</a> -&gt; Hierarchical multi-scale matching network for disparity estimation of high-resolution satellite stereo images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Sheng029/StereoMatchingRemoteSensing">StereoMatchingRemoteSensing</a> -&gt; Dual-Scale Matching Network for Disparity Estimation of High-Resolution Remote Sensing Images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://centreborelli.github.io/satnerf/" rel="nofollow">satnerf</a> -&gt; Learning Multi-View Satellite Photogrammetry With Transient Objects and Shadow Modeling Using RPC Cameras</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/WHU-GPCV/SatMVS">SatMVS</a> -&gt; Rational Polynomial Camera Model Warping for Deep Learning Based Satellite Multi-View Stereo Matching</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/prs-eth/ImpliCity">ImpliCity</a> -&gt; reconstructs digital surface models (DSMs) from raw photogrammetric 3D point clouds and ortho-images with the help of an implicit neural 3D scene representation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Sheng029/WHU-Stereo">WHU-Stereo</a> -&gt; a large-scale dataset for stereo matching of high-resolution satellite imagery &amp; several deep learning methods for stereo matching. Methods include StereoNet, Pyramid Stereo Matching Network &amp; HMSM-Net</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mikeroyal/Photogrammetry-Guide">Photogrammetry-Guide</a> -&gt; A guide covering Photogrammetry including the applications, libraries and tools that will make you a better and more efficient Photogrammetry development</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/mdmeadows/DSM-to-DTM">DSM-to-DTM</a> -&gt; Exploring the use of machine learning to convert a Digital Surface Model (e.g. SRTM) to a Digital Terrain Model</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Sheng029/GF-7_Stereo_Matching">GF-7_Stereo_Matching</a> -&gt; Large Scene DSM Generation of Gaofen-7 Imagery Combined with Deep Learning</p>
</li>

</li>

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Thermal Infrared</h2><a id="user-content-thermal-infrared" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šçƒ­çº¢å¤–" href="#thermal-infrared"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Thermal infrared remote sensing is a technique used to detect and measure thermal radiation emitted from the Earthâ€™s surface. This technique can be used to measure the temperature of the ground and any objects on it and can detect the presence of different materials. Thermal infrared remote sensing is used to assess land cover, detect land-use changes, and monitor urban heat islands, as well as to measure the temperature of the ground during nighttime or in areas of limited visibility.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/the-world-needs-a-lot-more-thermal-infrared-data-from-space-dbbba389be8a" rel="nofollow">The World Needs (a lot) More Thermal Infrared Data from Space</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.researchgate.net/publication/328400392_Object_Classification_in_Thermal_Images_using_Convolutional_Neural_Networks_for_Search_and_Rescue_Missions_with_Unmanned_Aerial_Systems" rel="nofollow">Object_Classification_in_Thermal_Images</a> -&gt; classification accuracy was improved by adding the object size as a feature directly within the CNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://chrieke.medium.com/thermal-imaging-with-satellites-34f381856dd1" rel="nofollow">Thermal imaging with satellites</a> blog post by Christoph Rieke</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">SAR</h2><a id="user-content-sar" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šSAR" href="#sar"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">SAR (synthetic aperture radar) is used to detect and measure the properties of objects and surfaces on the Earth's surface. SAR can be used to detect changes in terrain, features, and objects over time, as well as to measure the size, shape, and composition of objects and surfaces. SAR can also be used to measure moisture levels in soil and vegetation, or to detect and monitor changes in land use.</p>
<ul dir="auto">

<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">NDVI - vegetation index</h2><a id="user-content-ndvi---vegetation-index" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šNDVI - æ¤è¢«æŒ‡æ•°" href="#ndvi---vegetation-index"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) is an index used to measure the amount of healthy vegetation in a given area. It is calculated by taking the difference between the near-infrared (NIR) and red (red) bands of a satellite image, and dividing by the sum of the two bands. NDVI can be used to identify areas of healthy vegetation and to assess the health of vegetation in a given area. <code>ndvi = np.true_divide((ir - r), (ir + r))</code></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="http://nbviewer.jupyter.org/github/HyperionAnalytics/PyDataNYC2014/blob/master/ndvi_calculation.ipynb" rel="nofollow">Example notebook local</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/pangeo-data/pangeo-example-notebooks/blob/master/landsat8-cog-ndvi.ipynb">Landsat data in cloud optimised (COG) format analysed for NDVI</a> with <a href="https://medium.com/pangeo/cloud-native-geoprocessing-of-earth-observation-satellite-data-with-pangeo-997692d91ca2" rel="nofollow">medium article here</a>.</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jyamaoka/LandUse">Identifying Buildings in Satellite Images with Machine Learning and Quilt</a> -&gt; NDVI &amp; edge detection via gaussian blur as features, fed to TPOT for training with labels from OpenStreetMap, modelled as a two class problem, â€œBuildingsâ€ and â€œNatureâ€</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://medium.com/descarteslabs-team/seeing-through-the-clouds-34a24f84b599" rel="nofollow">Seeing Through the Clouds - Predicting Vegetation Indices Using SAR</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://towardsdatascience.com/how-to-compute-satellite-image-statistics-and-use-it-in-pandas-81864a489144" rel="nofollow">A walkthrough on calculating NDWI water index for flooded areas</a> -&gt; Derive zonal statistics from Sentinel 2 images using Rasterio and Geopandas</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/HaoZhang1018/NDVI-Net">NDVI-Net</a> -&gt; NDVI-Net: A fusion network for generating high-resolution normalized difference vegetation index in remote sensing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/px39n/Awesome-Vegetation-Index">Awesome-Vegetation-Index</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/rander38/Remote-Sensing-Indices-Derivation-Tool">Remote-Sensing-Indices-Derivation-Tool</a> -&gt; Calculate spectral remote sensing indices from satellite imagery</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">General image quality</h2><a id="user-content-general-image-quality" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šä¸€èˆ¬å›¾åƒè´¨é‡" href="#general-image-quality"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Image quality describes the degree of accuracy with which an image can represent the original object. Image quality is typically measured by the amount of detail, sharpness, and contrast that an image contains. Factors that contribute to image quality include the resolution, format, and compression of the image.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Achleshwar/lvrnet">lvrnet</a> -&gt; Lightweight Image Restoration for Aerial Images under Low Visibility</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/caiya55/jitter-compensation">jitter-compensation</a> -&gt; Remote Sensing Image Jitter Detection and Compensation Using CNN</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/VITA-Group/DeblurGANv2">DeblurGANv2</a> -&gt; Deblurring (Orders-of-Magnitude) Faster and Better</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/idealo/image-quality-assessment">image-quality-assessment</a> -&gt; CNN to predict the aesthetic and technical quality of images</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/hehaodong530/DOTA-C">DOTA-C</a> -&gt; evaluating the robustness of object detection models to 19 types of image quality degradation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/photosynthesis-team/piq">piq</a> -&gt; a collection of measures and metrics for image quality assessment</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/zhilin007/FFA-Net">FFA-Net</a> -&gt; Feature Fusion Attention Network for Single Image Dehazing</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/alexvbogdan/DeepCalib">DeepCalib</a> -&gt; A Deep Learning Approach for Automatic Intrinsic Calibration of Wide Field-of-View Cameras</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/richzhang/PerceptualSimilarity">PerceptualSimilarity</a> -&gt; LPIPS is a perceptual metric which aims to overcome the limitations of traditional metrics such as PSNR &amp; SSIM, to better represent the features the human eye picks up on</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/wenjiaXu/Optical-RemoteSensing-Image-Resolution">Optical-RemoteSensing-Image-Resolution</a> -&gt; Deep Memory Connected Neural Network for Optical Remote Sensing Image Restoration. Two applications: Gaussian image denoising and single image super-resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ImageRestorationToolbox/Hyperspectral-Deblurring-and-Destriping">Hyperspectral-Deblurring-and-Destriping</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Helmholtz-AI-Energy/HyDe">HyDe</a> -&gt; Hyperspectral Denoising algorithm toolbox in Python</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/Keiv4n/HLF-DIP">HLF-DIP</a> -&gt; Unsupervised Hyperspectral Denoising Based on Deep Image Prior and Least Favorable Distribution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/trile83/RQUNetVAE">RQUNetVAE</a> -&gt; Riesz-Quincunx-UNet Variational Auto-Encoder for Satellite Image Denoising</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/acecreamu/deep-hs-prior">deep-hs-prior</a> -&gt; Deep Hyperspectral Prior: Denoising, Inpainting, Super-Resolution</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/satellogic/iquaflow">iquaflow</a> -&gt; from Satellogic, an image quality framework that aims at providing a set of tools to assess image quality by using the performance of AI models trained on the images as a proxy.</p>
</li>
</ul>
<h1 dir="auto"></h1>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Synthetic data</h2><a id="user-content-synthetic-data" class="anchor-element" aria-label="æ°¸ä¹…é“¾æ¥ï¼šåˆæˆæ•°æ®" href="#synthetic-data"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Training data can be hard to acquire, particularly for rare events such as change detection after disasters, or imagery of rare classes of objects. In these situations, generating synthetic training data might be the only option. This has become quite sophisticated, with 3D models being use with open source games engines such as <a href="https://www.unrealengine.com/en-US/" rel="nofollow">Unreal</a>.</p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://arxiv.org/ftp/arxiv/papers/2001/2001.05130.pdf" rel="nofollow">The Synthinel-1 dataset: a collection of high resolution synthetic overhead imagery for building segmentation</a> with <a href="https://github.com/timqqt/Synthinel">repo</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://registry.opendata.aws/rareplanes/" rel="nofollow">RarePlanes</a> -&gt; incorporates both real and synthetically generated satellite imagery including aircraft. Read the <a href="https://arxiv.org/abs/2006.02963" rel="nofollow">arxiv paper</a> and checkout <a href="https://github.com/jdc08161063/RarePlanes">this repo</a>. Note the dataset is available through the AWS Open-Data Program for free download</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto">Read <a href="https://developer.nvidia.com/blog/preparing-models-for-object-detection-with-real-and-synthetic-data-and-tao-toolkit/" rel="nofollow">this article from NVIDIA</a> which discusses fine tuning a model pre-trained on synthetic data (Rareplanes) with 10% real data, then pruning the model to reduce its size, before quantizing the model to improve inference speed</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://one-view.ai/combining-synthetic-data-with-real-data-to-improve-detection-results-in-satellite-imagery-case-study/" rel="nofollow">Combining Synthetic Data with Real Data to Improve Detection Results in Satellite Imagery</a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/domlysz/BlenderGIS">BlenderGIS</a> could be used for synthetic data generation</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.bifrost.ai/" rel="nofollow">bifrost.ai</a> -&gt; simulated data service with geospatial output data formats</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.oktal-se.fr/deep-learning/" rel="nofollow">oktal-se</a> -&gt; software for generating simulated data across a wide range of bands including optical and SAR</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.iqt.org/synthesizing-robustness-yoltv4-results-part-1/" rel="nofollow">The Nuances of Extracting Utility from Synthetic Data</a> -&gt; We find that strategically augmenting the real dataset is nearly as effective as adding synthetic data in the quest to improve the detection or rare object classes, and that fully extracting the utility of synthetic data is a nuanced process</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://www.iqt.org/synthesizing-robustness/" rel="nofollow">Synthesizing Robustness</a> -&gt; explores how to best leverage and enhance synthetic data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://rendered.ai/" rel="nofollow">rendered.ai</a> -&gt; The Platform as a Service for Creating Synthetic Data</p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/yangxu351/synthetic_xview_airplanes"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">Synthesis_xview_airplanes</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; ä½¿ç”¨ ArcGIS CityEngine åˆ›å»ºé£æœºç»¼åˆæ•°æ®é›†</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://one-view.ai/combining-synthetic-data-with-real-data-to-improve-detection-results-in-satellite-imagery-case-study/" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å°†åˆæˆæ•°æ®ä¸çœŸå®æ•°æ®ç›¸ç»“åˆä»¥æ”¹å–„å«æ˜Ÿå›¾åƒçš„æ£€æµ‹ç»“æœï¼šæ¡ˆä¾‹ç ”ç©¶</font></font></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/FlorenceJiang/SynImageAnalysis"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">SynImageAnalysis</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; æ¯”è¾ƒæ½œåœ¨ç‰¹å¾ç©ºé—´ä¸­çš„åˆæˆå«æ˜Ÿå›¾åƒå’ŒçœŸå®å«æ˜Ÿå›¾åƒï¼ˆåµŒå…¥ï¼‰</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/ue4plugins/StreetMap"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">å°† OpenStreetMap æ•°æ®å¯¼å…¥è™šå¹»å¼•æ“ 4</font></font></a></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/RijulGupta-DM/deepfake-satellite-images"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">deepfake-satellite-images</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; åŒ…å«è¶…è¿‡ 100 ä¸‡å¼ åˆæˆèˆªç©ºå›¾åƒçš„æ•°æ®é›†</font></font></p>

<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/JakeForsey/synthetic-disaster"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">åˆæˆç¾éš¾</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">-&gt; ä½¿ç”¨æ·±åº¦ç¥ç»ç½‘ç»œç”Ÿæˆè‡ªç„¶ç¾å®³çš„åˆæˆå«æ˜Ÿå›¾åƒ</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/meidachen/STPLS3D"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">STPLS3D</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; å¤§è§„æ¨¡åˆæˆå’ŒçœŸå®èˆªç©ºæ‘„å½±æµ‹é‡ 3D ç‚¹äº‘æ•°æ®é›†</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/jianboqi/lessrt"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">LESS</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; å¼‚æ„3Dåœºæ™¯ä¸‹çš„å¤§è§„æ¨¡é¥æ„Ÿæ•°æ®å’Œå›¾åƒæ¨¡æ‹Ÿæ¡†æ¶</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://avanetten.medium.com/synthesizing-robustness-dataset-size-requirements-and-geographic-insights-a687192e8004" rel="nofollow"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">ç»¼åˆç¨³å¥æ€§ï¼šæ•°æ®é›†å¤§å°è¦æ±‚å’Œåœ°ç†æ´å¯Ÿ</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">-&gt; ä¸­å‹æ–‡ç« ï¼Œå¾—å‡ºçš„ç»“è®ºæ˜¯ï¼Œåˆæˆæ•°æ®å¯¹æœ€ç¨€æœ‰çš„å¯¹è±¡ç±»æœ€æœ‰åˆ©ï¼Œå¹¶ä¸”ä»åˆæˆæ•°æ®ä¸­æå–æ•ˆç”¨é€šå¸¸éœ€è¦ä»˜å‡ºå·¨å¤§çš„åŠªåŠ›å’Œåˆ›é€ åŠ›</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/gbaier/rs_img_synth"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">rs_img_synth</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; ä»åœŸåœ°è¦†ç›–å›¾å’Œè¾…åŠ©æ …æ ¼æ•°æ®åˆæˆå…‰å­¦å’Œ SAR å›¾åƒ</font></font></p>
</li>
<li>
<p dir="auto"><a href="https://github.com/naivelogic/OnlyPlanes"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;">OnlyPlanes</font></font></a><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"><font style="vertical-align: inherit;"> -&gt; è®ºæ–‡çš„æ•°æ®é›†å’Œé¢„è®­ç»ƒæ¨¡å‹ï¼šOnlyPlanes - Incrementally Tuning Synthetic Training Datasets for Satellite Object Inspection</font></font></p>
